# 5 Minute QuickStart | CoinKarma

![Page cover](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.unsplash.com%2Fphoto-1513569771920-c9e1d31714af%3Fcrop%3Dentropy%26cs%3Dsrgb%26fm%3Djpg%26ixid%3DM3wxOTcwMjR8MHwxfHNlYXJjaHw2fHxkYXJrfGVufDB8fHx8MTcyNDM3MzA2NHww%26ixlib%3Drb-4.0.3%26q%3D85&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cfd2d02&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/#limited-channel-jia-ru-hui-yuan-zhuan-shu-bin-dao-zhang-wo-ge-shi-kuai-xun)

🔈 Limited Channel｜加入會員專屬頻道 掌握各式快訊


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

以下頻道，為付費會員專屬限定，於[此頁面](https://www.coinkarma.co/account)
完成帳號綁定後，點擊導覽列 「 Telegram 機器人 」 即可加入。

*   📢 **Token Screener 山寨幣篩選器：於會員專屬頻道每小時播報，快速篩選出強勢幣種與弱勢幣種。**（詳細解說參考 [Token Screener](https://docs.coinkarma.co/features-guide/token-screener)
     頁面）
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FoNu4atQ5ro94Oojb6nL3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4943dadf-4be2-44e7-a36d-e7a370f525b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1d3511a&sv=2)

*   📢 **Market Pulse: 綜合指標指數，可即時觀測市場綜合狀況，把握行情反轉機會。**（詳細解說參考 [Market Pulse](https://docs.coinkarma.co/features-guide/market-pulse)
     頁面）
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FQ1cgtKBoN7zgosGBSe2B%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddd1f44a6-2275-4414-95f2-57f19a362408&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7d3c0b20&sv=2)

*   📢 **Overall Liquidity Alert**: 每小時播報，整合 BTC + ETH 的市值狀況與各幣種 LIQ 的狀態，以及市值加權 Overall LIQ 的實時數據。（詳細解說參考 [LIQ](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/liq)
     頁面）
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252F0fZ4XIBkgjaTHZZaIQOp%252FOverall%2520LIQ%2520chanel%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D775fc95e-6530-4d0b-b03d-e6fb12cc41ab&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e081ea01&sv=2)
    
    Overall LIQ 頻道參數說明
    
*   📢 **Grid Trading Signal**: 會員專屬 OKX 網格策略信號，根據 Overall LIQ 與幣種相對強弱指標，提供ㄧ鍵開單。（詳細解說參考 [Grid Trading Signal](https://docs.coinkarma.co/features-guide/grid-trading-signal)
     頁面）
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252F5ec7rdO0m8LCXe8oMTRx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8a83a47-9fcf-4e21-8df6-4dba9cd2feb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e163d057&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/#dashboard-overview-zhi-biao-kan-ban-shi-yong-jiao-xue)

📋 Dashboard Overview｜指標看板使用教學


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

註冊登入後，進入 CoinKarma 的 [Chart Dashboard](https://www.coinkarma.co/chart)
，即可觀測即時指標狀態並復盤歷史數據，以下是常見操作的快速指南：

*   **新增 CoinKarma 指標**：點擊 CoinKarma Indicator，選擇需要的指標項目（可選擇多個）
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FajJNjnRHN4SC3sc7LRRb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd84dbcf7-5298-4e48-b3b0-a991892f479a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ee975989&sv=2)

*   **調整參數 Benchmark**：滑鼠移至左下角指標名稱，點擊齒輪 icon，可調整參數值；點擊「Defaults」即可恢復預設值。
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FL1vkMeBFygzjVMQsSiks%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82605649-1135-4ffa-9ed8-942ea10f8553&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5e5b570d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/#indicators-tips-kuai-su-shang-shou-zhong-dian-zhi-biao)

🎯 Indicators Tips｜快速上手重點指標


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **精選指標概覽**
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252F2V7CAHYfEW6vyxxejlh6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fefdfdd-88bb-4b68-b7f1-61c4244ca16c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b16d074&sv=2)

*   **Overall LIQ**
    
    *   市值加權流動性指標，用於判斷市場整體流動性狀態。預設基準值為(2, -2)，低於-2 顯示紅柱，超過 2 顯示綠柱。建議與 CVD、Funding Rate、ARI 等指標綜合判斷。
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252F1PbjwahpzU1jmCUcvyfO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3713048c-c70f-45a1-bcb9-4e7b26c47b6a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e8979ba&sv=2)

*   **LIQ**
    
    *   單幣別流動性指標，輔助判斷個別幣種的流動性狀態。預設基準值為(3, -3)，低於-3 顯示紅柱，超過 3 顯示綠柱。不同幣種的 Benchmark 可自行調整，並與 Overall LIQ 及其他指標搭配使用。
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FqmHixitGv29IYpcu8Ktx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D893ebee3-4bc8-4d7a-b493-fb18cd01ef13&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2644091a&sv=2)

*   **ALT Resilient Index**
    
    *   Altcoins 抗跌指標，用於判斷在市場下跌趨勢中，Altcoins 相對於 BTC 的抗跌能力，數值越高，代表其在下跌中的強勢程度，適合用於判斷市場階段性低點。
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FJTLdVMOKrpIjOXX1odP5%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd94719fa-befc-4ed7-8657-be2481b07369&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7b28467e&sv=2)

*   **Accumulated Overall LIQ**
    
    *   為 Overall LIQ 的累積加總指標，可自行透過覆盤調整參數，預設值為（24, 70, -70），用於觀測過去 24 小時內 Overall LIQ 的數值加總，當超過 70 顯示綠柱，小於 -70 則為紅柱警示，適合搭配 Overall LIQ, ARI 等不同指尋找市場相對高低點的交易機會。
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FtDjR9B5b0uyrrMqqVtek%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e423836-1787-4bdc-88de-cf811ac84c4f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=888bf5d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/#referral-affiliates-yao-qing-hao-you-yu-lian-meng-tui-guang)

🤝 Referral & Affiliates｜邀請好友與聯盟推廣

登入 CoinKarma 後，點擊右上方個人頭像，進入「[Referral](https://www.coinkarma.co/account/referral)
」頁面，獲取專屬邀請連結，邀請好友加入 CoinKarma，您與好友均可獲得 CoinKarma Points，可用於使用期間的兌換延長。

若您是 KOL 或是擁社群資源，您的受邀獎勵將可直接兌換成美元現金，歡迎申請加入我們的 Affiliates Program ▶️ [申請表單（點我加入）](https://forms.gle/DXkodkvXrYhU6yiP8)

# 5 Minute QuickStart | English | CoinKarma

![Page cover](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fimages.unsplash.com%2Fphoto-1513569771920-c9e1d31714af%3Fcrop%3Dentropy%26cs%3Dsrgb%26fm%3Djpg%26ixid%3DM3wxOTcwMjR8MHwxfHNlYXJjaHw2fHxkYXJrfGVufDB8fHx8MTcyNDM3MzA2NHww%26ixlib%3Drb-4.0.3%26q%3D85&width=1248&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2cfd2d02&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english#limited-channel-join-exclusive-channels-for-real-time-updates)

🔈 Limited Channel｜Join Exclusive Channels for Real-Time Updates


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following channels are exclusively available to paid members. Link your account [here](https://www.coinkarma.co/account)
, then click the 「 Telegram Bot 」on navigation bar to join.

*   📢 **Token Screener**: A members-only channel that provides hourly updates, swiftly identifying the strongest and weakest performing tokens. (For more details, visit the [Token Screener page](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/token-screener)
    .)
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F33wgWkoEMN8aYrKS9UST%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df3aa6483-afae-4720-a453-0783305d1321&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8cffa9e6&sv=2)
    
*   📢 **Market Pulse**: A comprehensive market index offering real-time insights into overall market conditions—helping you catch trend reversals as they happen. (For more details, visit the [Market Pulse page](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/market-pulse)
    .)
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FZzrHyi7gqN6zHYPzNcd1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e63cfaf-c98f-4ceb-9799-6d51e6eec7e1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=daf6b4c4&sv=2)
    
*   📢 **Overall Liquidity Alert**: Broadcasts hourly updates on the market cap of BTC + ETH, the liquidity status of various coins, and real-time data of the market-cap-weighted Overall LIQ indicator.
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2FpSPhALa7CDgmj7otnbCE%2FOverall%2520LIQ%2520chanel.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e730f412&sv=2)
    
*   📢 **Grid Trading Signal**: A member-exclusive OKX grid trading strategy signal. It provides a one-click entry based on the Overall LIQ and the Relative Strength Indicator (RSI) of different coins. Exit positions need to be managed manually.
    
*   📢 **Set Custom Alert**: Set up custom indicator alerts. Receive real-time notifications when the set values are triggered.
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english#dashboard-overview-guide-to-using-the-indicator-dashboard)

📋 Dashboard Overview｜Guide to Using the Indicator Dashboard


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After registering and logging in, enter CoinKarma's [Chart Dashboard](https://www.coinkarma.co/chart)
 to observe real-time indicator statuses and review historical data. Here’s a quick guide to common operations

*   **Add CoinKarma Indicators**：Click on "CoinKarma Indicator" and select the desired indicators (you can choose multiple).
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2F28FMJ8fv0cIDaIYyPjOB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97a59cc&sv=2)

*   **Adjust Parameters (Benchmark)**：Hover over the indicator name in the bottom left, click the gear icon, and adjust the parameter values. Click "Defaults" to reset to the default values.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2F5DvC0MTGmG640Xta0g3n%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=75e69ce1&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english#indicators-tips-key-points-for-getting-started)

🎯 Indicators Tips｜Key Points for Getting Started


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Featured highlight indicators**
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FAoQNkTe7XuXeA5aPq3SK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82181d4-b018-4cab-ac3f-f0107c312543&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d62e310a&sv=2)
    
*   **Overall LIQ**
    
    *   A market-cap-weighted liquidity indicator used to gauge the overall market liquidity status. The default benchmark values are (2, -2), with red bars appearing when it falls below -2 and green bars above 2. It’s recommended to use this indicator along with CVD, Funding Rate, and ARI for a comprehensive analysis.
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2Fvh1lIMDSd4Ux0gD84vNT%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ccf7f36a&sv=2)
    
*   **LIQ**
    
    *   An individual coin liquidity indicator that helps assess the liquidity status of specific coins. The default benchmark values are (3, -3), with red bars below -3 and green bars above 3. You can adjust the benchmarks for different coins and combine them with Overall LIQ and other indicators.
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2Fft6bUy6kwETgzlf73MFN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51ee4af&sv=2)
    
*   **ALT Resilient Index**
    
    *   This is an altcoin resilience indicator, used to assess how altcoins hold up against BTC during market downturns. The higher the value, the stronger the altcoins perform during a decline. It’s useful for identifying potential market bottoms.
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2F9ynfcI0y1ouYD9ZOh14v%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae281544&sv=2)
    
*   **Accumulated Overall LIQ**
    
    *   A cumulative sum of the Overall LIQ indicator. You can adjust the parameters for backtesting, with default values set to (24, 70, -70). It tracks the sum of Overall LIQ over the past 24 hours, with green bars above 70 and red bars below -70, helping to spot potential trading opportunities at market highs and lows when combined with Overall LIQ, ARI, and other indicators.
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%2Fblobs%2F7ZF51OGtPhstucFR2kLX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a863c68b&sv=2)
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english#referral-and-affiliates-invite-friends-and-alliance-promotion)

# FAQs | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/getting-started/faqs#about-product-features)

**About Product Features**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Will too many users cause CoinKarma's alpha signals to become ineffective?**
    
    *   We will limit the number of members to maintain the effectiveness of the alpha signals and the quality of community interactions. In the first phase, the cap will be set between 1,000 to 2,000 members. Early members will benefit from a pricing advantage, and adjustments will be made later based on demand and pricing strategies.
        
    
*   **Will CoinKarma's LIQ indicator offer API services?**
    
    *   It's currently under planning. To protect the alpha signals, access will be limited to a set number of users.
        
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/getting-started/faqs#about-using-the-indicators)

About Using the Indicators


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **What's the difference between LIQ and Overall LIQ?**
    
    *   LIQ is the liquidity indicator for individual coins. For example, if you're charting BTCUSDT, it reflects BTC's liquidity. Overall LIQ is a market-cap-weighted liquidity indicator for the entire market. No matter which trading pair you're viewing, it will display the same data. In short, LIQ focuses on individual markets, while Overall LIQ provides a view of the entire market.
        
    
*   **How do I use the LIQ indicator in conjunction with position management for entering and exiting trades?**
    
    *   The LIQ indicator is more suitable for counter-trend trades in ranging markets. In a strong trending market, it may result in consecutive stop losses. You should adjust according to your own risk tolerance. For example, you could enter in batches: 10% of your position after the first green bar, another 10% after the fourth bar, or wait for the Accumulate LIQ (the sum of LIQ over the past 24 candlesticks) to reach a certain peak before entering.
        
    
*   **Since LIQ is a range-bound indicator, what should I do in a trending market?**
    
    *   You’ll need a filtering mechanism based on your trading preferences. A simple method would be using the 200-day moving average (MA) as a reference. If the price is above the 200 MA, you can use LIQ to filter for the best buying points. Below the 200 MA, be more cautious with long positions. You can also observe the Cumulative Volume Delta (CVD) to gauge the strength of a trend. Only when CVD continues to rise can the market potentially break through the sell pressure indicated by LIQ's red bars, and vice versa.
        
    
*   **How should I apply the LIQ indicator for different coins?**
    
    *   Given the high correlation in the crypto market, it's recommended to analyze both individual coin LIQ and Overall LIQ together to filter out meaningful buy and sell points.
        
    
*   **Some of my CoinKarma indicators are not displaying properly. How should I resolve this?**
    
    *   Try clearing your cache and cookies (hold Ctrl+Shift+R). If the problem persists, contact customer support.
        
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/getting-started/faqs#about-grid-and-quantitative-strategies)

About Grid and Quantitative Strategies


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **What is the selection logic behind the Grid Trading Signal?**
    
    *   Grid Trading Signal provides long or short signals when Overall LIQ hits certain thresholds. In addition to always having a BTC grid trade, it selects altcoins based on recent price performance—choosing stronger-performing coins for long trades and weaker-performing ones for short trades (ignoring individual coin LIQ).
        
    
*   **What are the stop-loss conditions for the Grid Trading Signal?**
    
    *   Each trade will be automatically closed if it incurs a 30% loss.
        
    
*   **Why did my Ultron copy trade fail to open a position?**
    
    *   Ultron tends to use smaller position sizes. The minimum position size for OKX is 0.001 BTC, so if your leverage-adjusted balance exceeds $12,000, the chance of failed orders decreases. If you're having trouble, try increasing your balance or leverage.
        
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/getting-started/faqs#other-information)

**Other Information**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have further questions, feel free to contact our support team via [https://t.me/CoinKarma\_Roman](https://t.me/CoinKarma_Roman)
, We'll do our best to assist you.

# Future Basis Rolling APY | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#what-is-future-basis-rolling-apy)

What is Future Basis Rolling APY?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FjO2aOuKs6XWPwD62sHCv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D728aeea5-7d8a-486a-9fb2-0cc03aee24f1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9db5b9fd&sv=2)

Future Basis Rolling APY refers to the annualized yield derived from the price difference (basis) between futures contracts and spot prices. In the crypto market, futures contracts for most coins often trade at a premium (positive basis) due to the market's long-term bullish sentiment. This creates an arbitrage opportunity.

**Arbitrage Opportunity Explained**

For example:

*   Suppose a BTC futures contract has a 2% price premium (basis) compared to the spot price, and the contract expires in 30 days.
    
*   An arbitrageur can **buy BTC in the spot market** and simultaneously **short the futures contract** for the same amount, locking in the 2% price difference.
    
*   By holding both positions until the contract expires, the arbitrageur secures the 2% profit as the prices converge, with minimal risk.
    

The annualized yield from this trade is calculated as: 2%\*(360/30)=24%

**Why "Rolling"?**

The term "Rolling" refers to the dynamic nature of this APY. As the contract approaches its expiration date, the basis narrows (converges with the spot price), and the APY changes. Traders often roll their positions to new contracts to maintain a steady yield.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#how-to-use-future-basis-rolling-apy)

How to Use Future Basis Rolling APY


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Indicator of Market Sentiment**

Just like the funding rate, Rolling APY reflects market sentiment. Higher premiums in futures contracts (and therefore higher APY) suggest optimism, while lower premiums signal fear or bearishness.

From historical data on BTC quarterly futures contracts, Rolling APY can be interpreted as follows:

*   **Below 0%:** Extreme pessimism (e.g., March 12, 2020, crash).
    
*   **0-5%:** Severe market fear.
    
*   **5-10%:** Neutral or calm market conditions.
    
*   **10-15%:** Slightly bullish sentiment.
    
*   **15-20%:** Market exuberance.
    
*   **Above 20%:** FOMO-driven speculation.
    

Default thresholds are typically set between **5% (neutral) and 20% (FOMO)**, but traders may adjust these based on backtesting and current market conditions.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#conclusion-future-basis-rolling-apys-limitations)

**Conclusion:** Future Basis Rolling APY's Limitations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Market Evolution and Data Sensitivity**
    
    *   Before BTC spot ETFs were approved, institutional investors had limited ways to gain exposure to Bitcoin, making futures contracts a key tool.
        
    *   With the introduction of ETFs, arbitrage between ETFs and futures has become easier, compressing the basis and muting Rolling APY values.
        
    
2.  **Adjusting Standards**
    
    *   Historical thresholds may no longer apply due to these changes.
        
    *   For instance, a Rolling APY of 15%-20% today may already indicate FOMO conditions, whereas it required 20%+ in the past.
        
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#conclusion)

Conclusion

Future Basis Rolling APY is a useful metric for understanding market sentiment and identifying arbitrage opportunities. However, as the market structure evolves, traders should regularly reevaluate thresholds and adapt their strategies accordingly. This indicator, when combined with others like funding rates, offers a clearer picture of the market’s state.

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

[PreviousALT resilient Index](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index)
[NextOI-Weighted Funding Rate](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [How to Use Future Basis Rolling APY](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#how-to-use-future-basis-rolling-apy)

# ALT resilient Index | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#what-is-the-ari-indicator-alt-resilient-index)

What is the ARI Indicator (ALT Resilient Index)?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdp3pS7y5T--z3FB7nSfr7Ykk6qGodOVkbTXKnt741GlVKjiB6xGa0kCfW0exK_00gHqxx2P-1evpqIfxKK-gtLFVhFJRuU7VARzkWnDhzZ7ARrwdnAbcAhDcaKHYdpviijgx8L9w%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a7525d90&sv=2)

The ARI (ALT Resilient Index) is designed to identify relatively safe entry points during market downturns by analyzing the behavior of altcoins compared to Bitcoin.

**Core Concept**

When Bitcoin (BTC) experiences significant declines but altcoins (ALT) do not follow suit with proportional drops, it often signals a short-term stabilization point. This phenomenon occurs because altcoins are generally more sensitive to selling pressure during market corrections. When the market begins to stabilize, market makers start accumulating the altcoins they previously sold, resulting in a rebound in the ALT/BTC ratio.

The ARI measures the willingness of market makers to absorb selling pressure during extreme market conditions. A higher ARI value indicates a stronger commitment by market makers to support prices, which often coincides with a market bottom.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#how-to-use-the-ari-indicator)

How to Use the ARI Indicator


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1\. Using ARI as a Standalone Entry Signal**

ARI is particularly effective during sharp corrections within bullish market trends, where Bitcoin often experiences drops exceeding 10-20%. During such corrections, the ARI indicator helps identify entry points with higher safety margins.

**Example:**

*   **Point A:** BTC correction due to "sell the news" after ETF approval.
    
*   **Point B:** Market turmoil caused by the intensifying Israel-Hamas conflict.
    
*   **Point C:** Japanese central bank's interest rate hike, triggering global financial turbulence.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FhP6u2oTtuEs8vJ2RQYGR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea660837-d3c1-4a10-9bfd-e7a4b1896481&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d02479a2&sv=2)

At each of these events, ARI highlighted relatively low-risk entry points during market fear.

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#id-2.-combining-ari-with-liq-for-enhanced-entry-strategies)

**2\. Combining ARI with LIQ for Enhanced Entry Strategies**

The ARI can be used alongside the LIQ (Liquidity Index) to filter entry signals during volatile markets.

**Example:** During the Bank of Japan's unexpected rate hike (July 31), Bitcoin dropped rapidly from 67K to 58K. The LIQ indicator generated an entry signal (yellow box), but the price continued to fall to a low of 49K. By incorporating ARI (orange box) as an additional filter, the safety margin of the entry was significantly improved.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252Fk3dUQbqTncY6qSDFntps%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59b4f712-1ba1-4a7a-9d4e-bb2366c376a9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=101952cc&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#conclusion-ari-indicators-strengths-and-limitations)

**Conclusion:** ARI Indicator's Strengths and Limitations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Strengths**

*   **Effective during sharp corrections:** The ARI excels in identifying safe entry points when the market experiences significant pullbacks.
    

**Limitations**

**Limited Trading Opportunities:** With a benchmark set at 3, ARI signals may trigger infrequently. Users can combine ARI with other indicators to maximize its utility.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FwXX2eagCLF1hnictDQoh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2614d1f6-0cce-4eed-bb80-b60c062ac3aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7bcc29b9&sv=2)

**Not Guaranteed to Pinpoint Absolute Lows:** While ARI reflects the willingness of market makers to absorb selling pressure, it does not account for all market-driving factors. For example: **January 2024:** During a "sell the news" event for Bitcoin, ARI triggered, but BTC still declined by over 10%. However, in hindsight, the ARI signal still indicated a solid entry zone.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FXGTESjZJz0y1PSg6a9sJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D665b5fd1-af69-4af1-a0fe-1acfa69a25fd&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ead862bc&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#conclusion)

Conclusion

The ARI indicator is a valuable tool for identifying high-safety-margin entry points during major corrections. While it excels in specific scenarios, combining it with other indicators like LIQ can enhance its effectiveness and mitigate its limitations. Users should always evaluate market dynamics holistically and recognize that no single indicator can account for all variables in the highly volatile crypto market.

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

# Karma Index | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/karma-index#what-is-the-karma-index)

**What Is the Karma Index?**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252Fu4xLki1gnSxrxbMPVORn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc05a6d03-59a9-4ed1-8181-7307517d1c28&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=403f23cc&sv=2)

The **Karma Index** is a comprehensive indicator designed to identify cyclical market tops and bottoms in cryptocurrency trading. It combines data from various sources, including:

*   **Spot market liquidity**
    
*   **On-chain metrics**
    
*   **Off-market sentiment**
    
*   **Exchange traffic**
    
*   **Derivatives market data**
    

By quantifying these factors, the Karma Index provides a reliable tool for traders to pinpoint the relative highs and lows of major market cycles.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/karma-index#the-challenge-defining-highs-and-lows)

**The Challenge: Defining Highs and Lows**

The fundamental strategy for success in trading is “**buy low, sell high.**” However, determining what constitutes “low” and “high” is the core challenge for any trader.

In an upward-trending market, each cycle tends to establish higher lows and higher highs.

*   **Low points** are defined as **cycle bottoms**, where sentiment is excessively bearish.
    
*   **High points** are **cycle tops**, characterized by market euphoria.
    

As the saying goes:

> _“Buy when there’s no interest, sell when there’s a frenzy.”_

Yet, these psychological turning points are notoriously difficult to act upon due to fear at the bottom and greed at the top.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/karma-index#features-of-the-karma-index)

**Features of the Karma Index**

The Karma Index stands out for its dual strengths:

1.  **Cyclical Awareness**: Accurately identifies the larger market cycles.
    
2.  **Precision**: Generates clear buy and sell signals that outperform other mainstream indicators.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/karma-index#how-to-use-the-karma-index)

**How to Use the Karma Index**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Karma Index is optimized for **long-term cycle analysis**, focusing on major market movements.

*   **Macro Cycle: The 2019–2021 Bull-Bear Cycle** During this cycle, even with the **March 12, 2020, event**, there was no panic selling of holdings. Instead, positions were steadily held until reaching the phase high in 2021.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F2SGIBV5YFsRhGrbfxUcG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6454b152-73e7-4f07-a7fa-aab2e9b5f9a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2535e3ce&sv=2)

*   **Within-Cycle: Accumulation Opportunities in the 2019–2021 Bull-Bear Cycle** Point B was a low in the Karma Index during this cycle and corresponded to Point A, which had the same Karma Index value. Afterward, BTC reached new highs. Looking back, Point B was at the tail end of consolidation following the **May 19 crash**, making it an excellent entry point.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcq_oItOQU8y_K-caPWcfWvw-jAe3DehkjIt7PtiLVui8rOqifOps2iCmLDAFwXQM_R3oM7-EWbaRYRa0o8CtWhcyOtvViItJCGmqxLC1i-c7wjf7z3ENOiJPk2Q_B9j5V3mxAcLw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98c01f05&sv=2)

*   **Macro Cycle: The 2022–2024 Bull-Bear Cycle** The **FTX bankruptcy event in November 2022** caused BTC to drop to a cycle low of 16K. During this period, the Karma Index provided a clear entry signal, enabling holders to ride the trend steadily to the phase high of 73K.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcVwhkxh0D6Vm1N2Uh20WPWPMCIN3vSlRqmglPSqYTUfiVIQuN2ISX9lAB4bKM5Xi-lkuS7CUGEn0VNamZp-VTeVN8OINUr905bQWNCyF5W2IheIdjEevaYmV23QLmc8ciwR1Bg6A%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9b1c4c81&sv=2)

*   **Within-Cycle: Accumulation Opportunities in the 2022–2024 Bull-Bear Cycle** Point B was a low in the Karma Index during this cycle and corresponded to Point A, which had the same Karma Index value. Afterward, BTC reached new highs. Looking back, Point B was precisely at the starting point of the Q4 bull market, making it an excellent entry point.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfBZGMQJVUKmNTT6PJuW31B19G8U-iOBAnJtg2qdb6e451bmHXdT2ZlsgIkSBCxa1hgeKmmj5oYQ-f0ZH79Tk6RTtpuS0yWVFsZVmJ8pB-Ftf82zsDXE1Ko3j-7cuAGFeIAsQeU%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3d20e1d4&sv=2)

* * *

**Cyclical Nature**

*   The **green arrows** in the historical chart represent **buy signals**, typically occurring at global cycle bottoms.
    
*   The **red arrows** indicate **sell signals**, correlating with cycle peaks.
    
*   The pattern demonstrates that frequent buy signals tend to align with bottoming phases, while sell signals coincide with market tops, validating the **cyclical reliability** of the index.
    

**Precision** Backtesting the Karma Index against other popular cyclical indicators—**AHR999** and **Crypto Greed & Fear Index**—reveals its superior accuracy in buy/sell signals.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FGVf5lTRbEHt6SpFRGorf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db67f2158-a2c3-4f9f-8e31-9561331ffa96&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b349c7f6&sv=2)

Allocate **10% of capital** on each buy signal, Close **50% of positions** on each sell signal.

# OI-Weighted Funding Rate | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#what-is-oi-weighted-funding-rate-open-interest-weighted-funding-rate)

What is OI-Weighted Funding Rate? (Open Interest-Weighted Funding Rate)


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcfRoNOwoVujyky-uXV_wJQD5FgElARc-CZeuO1OzlvpMlD_LhzJaqT7GBXJs_1Exn8uxqAJzjAG6l5uCmveKdJtJcKFrm79kJ5aiHAjzG-LNLrb32mT2DuUmXfJkuRUpmImWpxWw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28b575e0&sv=2)

The **OI-Weighted Funding Rate** is an adjusted metric that calculates the weighted average funding rate of BTC perpetual contracts across major exchanges, based on their open interest (OI). It provides a more comprehensive view of market sentiment by accounting for the relative size of positions on different platforms.

**Understanding Funding Rates**

Funding rates are a mechanism used by cryptocurrency exchanges to maintain the price of perpetual contracts in line with the underlying spot price. The funding rate typically consists of:

1.  **A constant interest rate (e.g., 0.01%)**, and
    
2.  **A premium component (based on price divergence).**
    

When perpetual contract prices trade significantly above the spot price:

*   **Funding rates increase** to make long positions more expensive.
    
*   This discourages excessive buying and incentivizes long positions to close, bringing prices back down.
    

Conversely, when perpetual contracts trade below the spot price:

*   **Funding rates turn negative**, making short positions costlier.
    
*   This incentivizes short positions to close, bringing prices back up.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#how-to-use-oi-weighted-funding-rate)

How to Use OI-Weighted Funding Rate


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Interpreting Market Sentiment**

Just like **Future Basis Rolling APY**, the OI-Weighted Funding Rate is an indicator of market sentiment.

1.  **When the funding rate surges** (indicating perpetual contracts are priced significantly higher than spot prices):
    
    *   Possible Scenarios:
        
        *   **Rising Trend:** Over-leveraged longs drive prices up as traders aggressively open bullish positions.
            
        *   **Falling Trend:** Long traders aggressively attempt to "buy the dip," pushing perpetual prices above spot levels.
            
        
    *   Implications for Bulls:
        
        *   High funding rates suggest euphoria, often driven by retail traders. Over-leveraged long positions may face liquidations, especially in a downturn.
            
        
    
2.  **When the funding rate drops** (indicating perpetual contracts are priced significantly lower than spot prices):
    
    *   Possible Scenarios:
        
        *   **Falling Trend:** Aggressive shorting with high leverage causes perpetual prices to fall below spot.
            
        *   **Rising Trend:** Bears continue shorting despite upward momentum, creating a divergence.
            
        
    *   Implications for Bears:
        
        *   High leverage among short positions makes them vulnerable to liquidations if the price moves upward.
            
        
    

**Market Behavior and Key Insights**

**High Funding Rates (Perpetual > Spot)**

*   **Bullish Overextension**
    
    *   A rising trend with high funding suggests optimism but often leads to volatility as leveraged long positions face liquidation risk.
        
    
*   **Bearish Reversal Potential**
    
    *   If funding spikes during a downtrend, it may indicate that longs are being squeezed, favoring shorts.
        
    

**Low Funding Rates (Perpetual < Spot)**

*   **Bearish Overextension**
    
    *   A falling trend with low funding indicates excessive pessimism, often driven by retail shorts.
        
    
*   **Bullish Reversal Potential**
    
    *   If funding plummets during an uptrend, it signals that shorts are over-leveraged, favoring longs.
        
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#conclusion-oi-weighted-funding-rates-limitations)

**Conclusion:** OI-Weighted Funding Rate's Limitations


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Like the **Future Basis Rolling APY**, the introduction of BTC spot ETFs and other regulated instruments has changed the market dynamics:

*   Institutional players can now easily hedge BTC exposure by shorting futures, compressing funding rates.
    
*   This **dampens funding rate volatility**, making historical thresholds less relevant.
    

**Example Adjustment:** Previously, a high funding rate (e.g., 0.1%+) signaled extreme euphoria. Today, lower values (e.g., 0.05%-0.08%) may already indicate over-leveraging.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#conclusion)

Conclusion

The OI-Weighted Funding Rate provides valuable insights into leverage dynamics and market sentiment. While it reflects extremes in bullish or bearish sentiment, evolving market structures require traders to recalibrate their thresholds and combine this indicator with others to improve accuracy.

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

# Bitfinex Indicators | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#what-are-bitfinex-indicators)

What Are Bitfinex Indicators?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F9RuCtEQ5D43Bq59vXGmN%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4569d140-fa1b-4b7c-b3cd-7ed015d902a4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26d6bfcd&sv=2)

Bitfinex Indicators are metrics designed to track the behavior of whales (large traders) on the Bitfinex exchange, providing insights into how these "smart money" players view the market. Bitfinex, a veteran cryptocurrency exchange operated by iFinex (also the parent company of Tether, issuer of USDT), is known for its significant whale activity that can influence market trends.

By monitoring these indicators, traders can gain valuable insights into market sentiment and identify potential opportunities during whale accumulation or distribution phases.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#how-to-usebitfinex-indicators)

How to Use**Bitfinex Indicators**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#bitfinex-btcusd-longs-bitfinex-ethusd-longs)

**Bitfinex BTCUSD LONGS / Bitfinex ETHUSD LONGS**

These indicators represent the total leverage-based long positions on BTC and ETH in BTC-denominated terms.

*   **Whale Behavior:** Whales often avoid aggressive market buys/sells due to their large capital size, which can cause price volatility. Instead:
    
    *   Whales **accumulate during price drops** (when sell-side liquidity is abundant).
        
    *   Whales **distribute during price rallies** (when buy-side liquidity is high).
        
    
*   **Application:**
    
    *   During sharp market declines, check whether whales are accumulating. For instance, during the 2022 bear market, BTC dropped below $35K after the LUNA collapse, prompting significant whale buying that lasted until $16K.
        
    *   Watch for whales completing their distribution phases. For example, by March 2024, whales had offloaded most of their positions established during the 2022 bear market. Following BTC's peak of $73K, the market entered a prolonged consolidation phase, with BTC dipping below $50K in August 2024 before whales resumed accumulation.
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FQpI3TL7E9zBaom5bfeWV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ee0e12d-3b97-4dff-8cd4-f091ea437f59&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3fd8ac&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#bitfinex-margin-long-size)

**Bitfinex Margin Long Size**

This indicator measures the total leveraged USD/USDT borrowing positions on Bitfinex.

*   **Relationship with BTCUSD LONGS:** Similar to BTCUSD LONGS, it reflects whale behavior during accumulation and distribution phases. However, it tends to exhibit **greater sensitivity**, making it a useful early warning indicator.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252Fba8Yh1zXCyhGYi0JnJqX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd281406c-d08f-4bf3-a95b-98f5e38f4ffb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8a368897&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#bitfinex-premium)

**Bitfinex Premium**

The Bitfinex Premium compares BTCUSD prices on Bitfinex versus Coinbase.

*   **Interpretation:**
    
    *   When **Bitfinex BTCUSD is at a premium to Coinbase**, it indicates bearish sentiment, with whales accumulating during downturns.
        
    *   When **Bitfinex BTCUSD trades at a discount to Coinbase**, it signals bullish sentiment, as whales offload positions during uptrends.
        
    
*   **Threshold Example:**
    
    *   Premium/Discount exceeding ±0.25% often coincides with market tops or bottoms.
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252Fh5N9YDulXhYoGC2mrL2D%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De617c9ef-5767-4fec-ae78-d814e7f94095&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c7f5801&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#bitfinex-eth-btc-whale-indicator)

**Bitfinex ETH/BTC Whale Indicator**

This indicator tracks the net long leveraged positions in ETH/BTC pairs.

*   **Interpretation:**
    
    *   A high indicator value suggests whales are borrowing BTC to long ETH, indicating bullish ETH sentiment relative to BTC.
        
    *   Conversely, a decline in this indicator signals whales closing ETH longs, often coinciding with ETH/BTC exchange rate peaks.
        
    
*   **Application:**
    
    *   Example: After whales closed significant ETH/BTC long positions, the ETH/BTC ratio often peaked, signaling a potential shift from ETH to BTC as a safer allocation.
        
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252Fh38z76bt1Q1ONyWJff0h%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D431f232a-900b-4a09-bae6-9d86bf268020&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=23cd61e6&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#conclusion-bitfinex-indicatorss-strengths-and-limitations)

**Conclusion: Bitfinex Indicators**'s Strengths and Limitations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Best Use Cases:**

*   These indicators are ideal for **medium to long-term market analysis**.
    
*   They help traders understand whale behavior and market sentiment trends over longer cycles.
    

**Limitations:**

*   Whale trading strategies on Bitfinex involve **large-scale, prolonged accumulation and distribution**, making these indicators less effective for short-term or intraday trading.
    
*   As a result, retail traders should combine Bitfinex Indicators with other CoinKarma tools and indicators to refine their strategies.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#conclusion)

**Conclusion**

Bitfinex Indicators provide a unique perspective into the behavior of smart money, helping traders align their strategies with whale sentiment. While they are less suitable for short-term trades, these metrics can offer valuable insights into broader market cycles when used alongside other analysis tools.

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

# Exchange App iOS Ranking | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/exchange-app-ios-ranking#what-is-the-exchange-app-ios-ranking)

What is the Exchange App iOS Ranking?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The iOS App Ranking tracks download rankings of centralized exchange apps in the U.S. market.

During quiet market periods, many people gradually exit the market, resulting in decreased attention. However, when the market enters a frenzy, hearing stories of others making money draws people back in droves—even those with no prior interest, like kids shining shoes, seek ways to enter the market. This phenomenon is commonly referred to as the "Shoeshine Boy Effect."

By observing the download rankings of the Coinbase app, it’s possible to gauge whether the Shoeshine Boy Effect is occurring. When the app ranks among the top few, it signifies a highly exuberant market with widespread interest in joining, and vice versa.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/exchange-app-ios-ranking#how-to-use-the-exchange-app-ios-ranking)

How to Use the Exchange App iOS Ranking


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The blue line in the indicator represents Coinbase’s ranking within the Finance category of iOS apps in the U.S. A lower value indicates a higher rank. When the Coinbase app climbs higher in the rankings, it reflects a stronger retail interest in crypto in the U.S. market. If the app ranks within the Top 10, surpassing traditional finance apps like Interactive Brokers or Yahoo Finance, it could signal a short-term overheated market, as most retail participants have already entered.

Looking back at past bull markets, when Coinbase consistently ranked in the Top 10 for an extended period, it often marked a local market top. The longer the rankings stayed elevated, the more likely it was that the trend was approaching a global peak. The chart below uses a Top 10 threshold as a reference, reviewing the bull markets of 2021 and 2024 for readers’ insights.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FTDlTB5XucDXC9HtK2PLs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0e49c6a-11b9-4ea0-86ad-4a617693d28c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fa7f7fee&sv=2)

# Binance Insurance Fund | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#what-is-the-binance-insurance-fund-contract-risk-protection-fund)

What is the Binance Insurance Fund (Contract Risk Protection Fund)?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

According to Binance's documentation:

**Definition**

The Contract Risk Protection Fund is a safeguard mechanism designed to limit the impact of counterparty liquidations. It protects traders from adverse losses caused by bankrupt positions and ensures that profits from winning positions are fully paid out to the profitable traders.

**Source of Funds**

When a position is liquidated, unless the position becomes a bankrupt one after liquidation, the remaining assets (after deducting the portion required to maintain the position) are charged as liquidation fees by Binance. A portion of these fees is allocated to the Contract Risk Protection Fund.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#key-insights)

Key Insights

Perpetual contracts operate as a zero-sum market: for every gain, there is a corresponding loss. During extreme market conditions, if the losing side's margin is insufficient to fully cover the profits of the winning side, the Binance Insurance Fund steps in to make up the difference. Therefore, the Insurance Fund typically decreases only after extreme leveraged liquidations occur.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#how-to-use-the-binance-insurance-fund)

How to Use the Binance Insurance Fund


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Binance Insurance Fund tends to grow steadily over time. It decreases only during events of massive liquidations that result in user bankruptcies. When the Insurance Fund decreases, it indicates excessive short-term liquidations have occurred.

This is particularly effective when analyzing leveraged long positions:

*   A decrease in the Binance Insurance Fund often suggests a market that has been excessively cleared out, which may signal a **short-term bottom**.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F5YiLmyBeiLmau6Dp8N1G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D498a2652-666f-476a-8f61-61a86f433e89&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e28a74ec&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

# USD/USDT Interest Rate | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate#what-is-the-usd-usdt-interest-rate)

What is the USD/USDT Interest Rate?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In addition to crypto-native features like perpetual contracts and funding rates, the crypto market also includes borrowing interest rates commonly seen in traditional finance. These rates are generated by spot borrowing activities on centralized exchanges. There are two key elements to analyze: the centralized exchange and the interest rate levels. Currently, the benchmark data comes from Binance, the world’s largest exchange, and Bitfinex, a long-standing platform renowned for lending activities.

**● Binance**

As the world’s largest exchange, Binance has a more diverse user base, with a relatively high proportion of retail traders. This composition often leads to more aggressive behavior during periods of price discovery or bull markets.

**● Bitfinex**

Bitfinex, one of the oldest exchanges, is characterized by its seasoned user base, often consisting of crypto-native whales. Observing Bitfinex’s borrowing interest rates can provide insights into how so-called “smart money” perceives current market conditions.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate#how-to-use-the-usd-usdt-interest-rate)

How to Use the USD/USDT Interest Rate


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The USD/USDT Interest Rate is a highly cyclical indicator. Given the differing characteristics and user bases of the two exchanges, Binance’s borrowing behavior is viewed as representative of retail traders, while Bitfinex’s behavior reflects that of market movers.

Key observations:

*   When **Bitfinex’s borrowing rate > Binance’s borrowing rate**, it often signals a market bottom.
    
*   When **Bitfinex’s borrowing rate < Binance’s borrowing rate**, it often signals a market top.
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate#disclaimer)

# Stablecoin Supply | English | CoinKarma

What is Stablecoin Supply?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stablecoin Supply refers to the circulating market capitalization of stablecoins such as USDT and USDC.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#how-to-use-stablecoin-supply)

How to Use Stablecoin Supply


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#by-comparing-the-market-capitalization-of-the-largest-stablecoin-usdt-with-the-price-of-btc)

By comparing the market capitalization of the largest stablecoin, USDT, with the price of BTC:

• In 2022, as the market declined, USDT’s market cap also decreased → indicating funds flowing out of the market and a continuous reduction in market liquidity.

• Conversely, as the market began to recover in 2023-2024, USDT’s market cap increased → signaling funds flowing into the market and a steady increase in market liquidity.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXepJcCldLtoXiLwYqWpgsHegk4GW8g8aOKrtbLG33-nECvw7hOmtAr7rvxaWte5eQgfGvj6F24u2QGWIsTRexG5rSoiPHudrcm0L7tEIZ3EB7n-6dLzQB7ccXa644mIuaiP9waysQ%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58c566fb&sv=2)

Key Observation: USDC’s Counter-Trend Issuance

Analysis reveals that when USDC experiences counter-trend issuance, diverging from price movements, it may signal a market bottom. For example:

• When Overall LIQ shows green bars combined with a USDC issuance exceeding $1 billion, this often forms a short-term range bottom in the market.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcsbvGJaYjL1JXDvyGe3A_GlDis_J6rI5p3FzDDx8DnHHRaSG0kEQT6sodHXPb6P0gniZtYqSDWkadxBMw9F37H1OBggdhaB3m5qnTu6awt2LicaszU67YKN-AYci-f6njXwvj9hA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8baf7e54&sv=2)

# BTC ETF Net Flow | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#what-is-btc-etf-net-flow)

What is BTC ETF Net Flow?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC ETF Net Flow measures the net inflows (or outflows) of U.S.-listed BTC ETFs. CoinKarma tracks the daily net flow data for 10 BTC ETFs traded in the U.S. market.

CoinKarma includes this indicator because historical analysis reveals that a portion of BTC ETF inflows originates from arbitrage trades, which have limited direct impact on price trends. This challenges the intuitive notion that net inflows signal bullishness, while net outflows signal bearishness. Instead, BTC ETF Net Flow can provide insights into sentiment in the futures market.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#how-to-use-btc-etf-net-flow)

How to Use BTC ETF Net Flow


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following illustrates how U.S. investors use BTC ETFs for arbitrage:

*   **When market sentiment is bullish (overheated):** Futures premiums rise, prompting arbitrage traders to buy BTC ETFs while shorting CME futures.
    
*   **When market sentiment is bearish (fearful):** Futures premiums decline, leading arbitrage traders to sell BTC ETFs and close their CME shorts.
    

**Observation:** At market tops, CME open interest typically spikes (corresponding to hedge funds increasing net short positions). After sharp market corrections, CME open interest declines alongside the market.

These arbitrage traders don’t need to wait until futures expire to close their positions. They profit by shorting during market FOMO and closing their shorts during panic sell-offs as market sentiment oscillates.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#ibit-and-arbitrage-behavior)

IBIT and Arbitrage Behavior

IBIT, due to its investor profile and lower fees, is particularly favored by arbitrage traders. While other ETFs exhibit similar behavior, their scale is far smaller compared to IBIT. By comparing IBIT’s net flows with BTC price movements, we observe that:

*   **Net outflows or a halt in inflows of IBIT funds** (indicating short positions being closed and ETF holdings being sold) often coincide with **short-term market bottoms**.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FeGVEel6hCXR990FUtxZW%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacbffe04-99d7-4ff4-8615-1703d4748edf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4e44d9d8&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#disclaimer)

# CVD(Cumulative Volume Delta) | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#what-is-cvd-cumulative-volume-delta)

What is CVD (Cumulative Volume Delta)?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CVD is an indicator used to analyze the balance of buying and selling pressure in the market. It accumulates the volume difference between buy and sell orders over a given time period.

In simple terms, CVD reflects the "market order" buying and selling strength during a specific trend.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#why-does-coinkarma-include-the-cvd-indicator)

Why Does CoinKarma Include the CVD Indicator?

CoinKarma features CVD because its LIQ-related indicators are based on bid (buy) and ask (sell) orders from the spot order book—essentially composed of "limit orders." However, when "market orders" consistently drive price movement in one direction during a trend, they can deplete most of the "limit orders," causing LIQ-related data to show excessive extension.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#how-to-use-cvd)

How to Use CVD


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This section focuses on comparing CVD with instances of LIQ overextension to demonstrate how CVD can filter out such scenarios.

**Example:** In cases where Overall LIQ red bars appear excessively (as marked by the yellow boxes), prices often continue to reach new highs. Observing the CVD during these periods reveals strong market buying activity, which consumes a significant amount of sell (ask) limit orders. This depletion leads to LIQ overextension.

By analyzing CVD, traders can identify these scenarios and avoid taking short positions during such periods.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FYHsS4cZ2Y0luhQI8kaOb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8596955-23fc-488a-a963-eca249274d30&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a623a3b7&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#disclaimer)

# LSUR Z Index | English | CoinKarma

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/lsur-z-index#shen-mo-shi-lsurzindex)

What is the LSUR Z Index

The LSUR Z Index represents the weighted LSUR (Long/Short User Ratio) of major cryptocurrencies based on open interest, measured in terms of how many standard deviations it deviates from its 14-day average. For example, a value of -2 means it’s two standard deviations below the average.

(_Note: LSUR refers to the ratio of long to short positions in perpetual futures contracts._)

Historically, in the crypto market, an LSUR below 1 indicated that more traders were shorting than longing—typically a sign of overly pessimistic market sentiment. This often marked a potential market bottom, making it a common short-term reversal signal. However, in recent years, this relationship has broken down or even reversed. An LSUR below 1 can now sometimes precede short-term market tops.

The exact reason remains unclear, but CoinKarma hypothesizes that the structural shift is due to the influx of institutional capital and their hedging strategies. Unlike retail investors, institutions often hold large spot positions and hedge them by opening short positions in futures—not necessarily because they’re bearish, but as a risk management tactic. As a result, an LSUR below 1 may no longer reflect extreme bearish sentiment, but rather strategic positioning.

Despite these changes, LSUR still provides valuable insights. Using CoinKarma’s proprietary algorithms, the LSUR Z Index remains a useful tool for gauging short-term market direction.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/lsur-z-index#ru-he-yun-yong-lsurzindex)

How to use LSUR Z Index

The LSUR Z Index is best interpreted in conjunction with other CoinKarma indicators. Examples include:

● Spotting Potential Reversal Points with Overall LIQ

In a ranging market, when the LSUR Z Index and Overall LIQ show aligned signals, it can indicate a possible trend reversal.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeiUAmf97NCa1gCl_ACrqQpjjK7oAA1erinkCVILwnsmJEdZAQNSsoXdXaU6pAz_CkNZghr-_TZuS66-QM7c-L3KvJBYQa86A9lxLMh49GrXLz8SEoCwf9xIGzrm1wamx8fxx0kPw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd27ac76&sv=2)

● Identifying Overextended Conditions with LIQ Indicators

*   Yellow Box: When both LIQ-related indicators and the LSUR Z Index suggest a potential pullback but the price remains strong, this implies that previously effective reversal signals are weakening. This could be a sign that the market is transitioning from range-bound to trending, and shorting should be avoided.
    
*   Purple Box: When the LSUR Z Index drops below -2, use it alongside LIQ indicators to filter out noise and avoid making decisions based solely on LSUR Z Index readings.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeXR3hDJmv7QVoxYa_QSB-qZotxhDFoC9k7WMFXVgMu-dHelxpun4lUFYbGQKlKE5PSZj-WofTz3tkOl-2I8SrnrpHx8ktIAdu6u2DevrfX4OKZhyrR_JWMST6_nnjfd2e2awBq%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1e51eca4&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/lsur-z-index#disclaimer)
