# LIQ | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#what-is-the-liq-indicator)

What is the LIQ Indicator?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfckYrou_5nKpoDakAAa3ZEB4qI9lubNoPqQQX6oSPdHP11ellqrKbVRYoSVcbIU9LV2d0SacKg77-Kt61_LoJmBJa578wcSGXz9tXz4jo52wfj07YJMPh8uS26oBR_uxhv-hKEMw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84b62246&sv=2)

_The red and green arrows on the chart correspond to the LIQ indicator_

Before diving into the mechanics of the LIQ indicator, it’s essential to understand the factors influencing the cryptocurrency market:

**Long-Term Factors:**

These drive external capital inflows and outflows in the crypto market, determining whether a directional "trend market" develops.

*   **BTC Adoption Rate:** The percentage of people outside the crypto space recognizing BTC as a valuable asset. For example, Bitcoin ETFs being approved in 2024.
    
*   **Overall Monetary Market Liquidity:** Factors like U.S. interest rate hikes or cuts, and the expansion or contraction of the balance sheets of major central banks.
    
*   **Crypto-Specific Trends:** Topics that attract external capital, such as DeFi, NFTs, or ICOs.
    

**Short-Term Factors:**

Short-term market movements are primarily driven by "high-leverage liquidations," leading to a volatile, range-bound market.

*   **High Leverage in Derivatives Markets:** Crypto retail investors tend to use high leverage in contracts, making derivatives markets a key tool for market makers to "harvest" retail positions. Hence, short-term price movements are often influenced by derivatives data.
    
*   **Market Maker Perspective:** Market makers evaluate the cost of manipulating prices to liquidate leveraged positions versus the potential profit. They will only act if the potential gains significantly outweigh the costs.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#what-is-liq)

**What is LIQ?**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LIQ is an indicator designed to analyze movements in a volatile market. Below is a detailed breakdown of its logic:

**Core Logic:**

LIQ is a standardized indicator calculated using the ratio of quantities in the spot order book.

*   **Order Book Composition:** Comprised of buy orders (_bids_) and sell orders (_asks_).
    
*   **CoinKarma's Proprietary Algorithm:** Standardizes calculations to identify price ranges where the cost of upward or downward movement for market makers is higher.
    

**Interpretation Logic:**

The LIQ indicator helps assess the cost of upward (_buy up_) or downward (_sell down_) price manipulation by market makers.

*   **High LIQ (>3):** Indicates deeper buy orders in the lower order book. This means it’s costlier for market makers to push the price down, suggesting a likely bottom in a volatile market.
    
*   **Low LIQ (<-3):** Indicates deeper sell orders in the upper order book. This makes it costlier for market makers to push the price up, suggesting a likely top in a volatile market.
    

In simple terms, the LIQ indicator reveals the cost of market maker manipulations. When the cost of price control becomes too high, market reversals are more likely.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#how-to-use-the-liq-indicator)

**How to Use the LIQ Indicator**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#using-liq-alone-to-identify-entry-points)

**Using LIQ Alone to Identify Entry Points**

If we define the price movements within the white box as a large volatile range, LIQ effectively marks both the range's bottom and top. (Benchmarks: +3, -3)

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeHKlGtknc8Dk3Lc_Em0SmfJeuXRFhSBdtGKtPEagNdC60MODJqYFYGyvdso_FQSI4XIlkQb3mI92mVnPBXkGHxkBnbvOLUMUwmdhn2MN26BqN3STqXS1MR42yrwwZuNUsj6b9-4g%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b52d13d2&sv=2)

*   **Chart Behavior:**
    
    *   _Green Arrows:_ Appear when Overall LIQ > 2 and BTC LIQ > 3.
        
    *   _Red Arrows:_ Appear when Overall LIQ < -2 and BTC LIQ < -3.
        
    

**Example:**

*   After the first green arrow appears in a volatile market, there’s often still significant distance to the actual bottom. This is due to the crypto derivatives market's natural long bias, making liquidating long positions more profitable. Even if the cost of pushing prices lower is high, market makers may continue to do so.
    
*   Conversely, after the first red arrow, the distance to the top is usually shorter than the green arrow's distance to the bottom. Therefore:
    
    *   When green bars appear, gradually build long positions.
        
    *   When red bars appear, close positions more promptly.
        
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#using-cvd-as-an-alert-for-overextended-liq)

**Using CVD as an Alert for Overextended LIQ**

LIQ is based on order book (limit order) data (_bids_ and _asks_). However, when market buy pressure (reflected in rising CVD) is strong, it can cause LIQ to overextend. CVD can be used to filter out trending markets, avoiding short positions in a strongly upward market.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXezJsotSn0ss729N2crgeaRSGpggXn5qjebd6h_IvNOpi-VmNCBSq7unyQsKByFeDdwkTIMsWuXzBRqf8d7-Ef2zkVDTpI5uSo4dQF41m-ierpmBc5bYnNR4MrdF6hkzEPk-iBKBA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=959a7f2e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#combining-liq-with-other-coinkarma-indicators)

**Combining LIQ with Other CoinKarma Indicators**

CoinKarma develops multiple indicators to complement LIQ for better trade strategies.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXczQs6SMtiRla780_3RkdrZiZD0_9GMXNyI6tvo5ca-bHpLidJsmmrjdCK42L7Iv3vaEFzyVZRylcxVO0gbMiwDH8H5jLdliG9Gj3SWoogzc-LEGD0Ot9qYFdvGYK1Q__qxI1OvLQ%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b6adebc4&sv=2)

Examples:

1.  **LIQ + LIQ Accumulated:** Stricter entry/exit conditions, though trading opportunities are fewer.
    
    *   Purple box: LIQ; Yellow box: LIQ + LIQ Accumulated.
        
    
2.  **LIQ + ALT Resilient Index:** Similar stricter strategy for entries/exits.
    
    *   Purple box: LIQ; Yellow box: LIQ + ALT Resilient Index.
        
    

By backtesting with various configurations, users can build LIQ-based trading strategies.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#liq-derived-indicators)

**LIQ-Derived Indicators**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#overall-liq)

**Overall LIQ**

*   **Principle:** Same as LIQ but weighted by market cap, representing overall market liquidity.
    
*   **Difference:** LIQ focuses on a single asset (e.g., BTC/USDT), while Overall LIQ represents the broader market, showing the same data across all trading pairs.
    

Overall LIQ is a market cap-weighted liquidity indicator that reflects the overall liquidity of the market. No matter which trading pair you’re viewing, the data shown remains consistent. In simple terms, LIQ focuses on a single market, while Overall LIQ provides a broader view of the entire market.

Currently, the coins included in CoinKarma’s Overall LIQ are:

(BTCUSDT, BTCUSD, ETHUSDT, ETHUSD, XRPUSDT, SOLUSDT, DOGEUSDT, ADAUSDT, AVAXUSDT, DOTUSDT, LINKUSDT, BCHUSDT, NEARUSDT, PEPEUSDT)

*   **Application:** Combine LIQ with Overall LIQ for more sensitive and frequent short-term trading signals.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXe82xXlx0tsiU91qIgV83guHMXBKOQ9_sRkBm6CMBoDMk78CfM9zLW0yiekDf-dsi11iZy9H2HdxUoIFnF4Ayt0sK3_HBNuW0QS6JUxZJo7GJw6_22AaPaTugiKowCIrFj1swV4fA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=792cccd2&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#accumulated-liq)

**Accumulated LIQ**

*   **Principle:** Adds a time dimension to LIQ by accumulating past values.
    
*   **Application:**
    
    *   1-hour time frame: Default settings (24, 60, -60).
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXe_bDaJYM1EjEue9vr_FQchQ9p6WKjbEEFdjWNeXIGVJ6Ghs8IFI8UIO1Egr4R0RHmQFUPKKWLSvahLBDnvqgYTh74rYSkTwZ3EXwtiJRSOia--eM0CKgN0N_1MXiWMuDvhUpuZ5Q%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b2f9683&sv=2)
    
    *   4-hour time frame: Default settings (50, 100, -100).
        
    
    ![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXejJn-cZP3-_JAeIAuyo26YJFbQCb-P2kgBn-wVWmhpOSt9Rnjx9oZsgEvqV_LeigbEFmqdUs6v9Ax6o98gKnxfgZoq86iWjKt9k-lxySw0djaM4VSEBHcxQzPMfH1quU2kKekxaA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72f38753&sv=2)
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#id-10-orderbook-dif)

**10% Orderbook DIF**

*   **Principle:** Measures the difference in bid-ask within the top 10% of the order book.
    
*   **Application:** Helps gauge the liquidity strength of buyers or sellers under identical LIQ conditions.
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc92vq2XnDd1ZH397fSyH8Cm4TdNlhr9gteACSGk88VwqdyR9aoSZoFwSbKcRzVcmQZBWNGhmD3ZCZDPx7FnZpr2FGmRb-c5ulQKX-A6BX4KgVuJ1MA7Ed0wENm4o2i8qM7IO6T%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=593c42f3&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#id-10-overall-liquidity)

10% Overall Liquidity

Concept: The metric is based on the difference between bids and asks within 10% of the overall market order book. ([Referencing the coins currently included in CoinKarma’s Overall LIQ.](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/liq#overall-liq)
)

Application: By analyzing the 10% Overall Liquidity, we can observe that—given the same Overall LIQ values—buy-side liquidity in the yellow box is greater than that in the purple box. (Default thresholds are set at 300 million and -300 million.)

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FeMijOlPnKf9n2QElhaJi%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db94a8d3b-0209-42d7-a761-0a758bb5a148&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=38473adc&sv=2)

Overall Liquidity – Displayed in BTC: You can choose to display liquidity in BTC through the indicator settings. (Default thresholds: +3000 BTC, -3000 BTC.)

The logic behind it is: the difference between bids and asks within 10% of the overall market order book, divided by the current BTC price. In a bullish scenario, backtesting has shown that this metric has strong predictive value for price movements.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FKcZuKr1bAkjX23GHRJ9e%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D93a58b55-7400-41a5-8af3-fb52e2cba0e5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=20a7635b&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#conclusion-liqs-strengths-and-limitations)

**Conclusion: LIQ's Strengths and Limitations**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Applicable Scenarios**

LIQ performs best during range-bound markets with no significant capital inflows or outflows.

**Limitations**

1.  **Trend Markets:** LIQ struggles during strong directional trends, as seen in November 2024 when external capital pushed BTC from $67K to $99K.
    
2.  **Macro Factors:** Events like aggressive interest rate hikes in 2022 caused large capital outflows, reducing LIQ's effectiveness.
    
3.  **Asset-Specific Thresholds:** Different assets may require adjusted LIQ benchmarks due to varying market-making styles. Users can fine-tune settings for better accuracy.
    

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/liq#disclaimer)

# CME Smart Money | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money#what-is-cme-smart-money)

What is CME Smart Money?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In the market, certain whales have enough holdings to significantly influence prices. When these entities buy, they provide strong buying support. Beyond their market impact, information asymmetry has always been a cornerstone of profitability in trading. Observing whales that likely possess this informational edge can help forecast potential market trends.

In 2024, around the approval of the BTC ETF, the market narrative largely revolved around this event. During that period, the Chicago Mercantile Exchange (CME) became the most accessible platform for U.S. traditional financial traders to trade BTC.

CME Smart Money is an indicator derived by identifying specific groups of traders on CME whose position changes have historically shown alpha in market trends.

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money#how-to-use-cme-smart-money)

How to Use CME Smart Money


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Unit:** Contracts; one contract equals 5 BTC.
    
*   **Reading:** Above the zero line indicates net long positions; below the zero line indicates net short positions.
    
*   **Update Cycle:** Data updates every Saturday (UTC+8), reflecting the positions as of the preceding Tuesday.
    

From 2022 to 2023, whenever CME Smart Money shifted to a net short position, it often marked a local market top.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F7WTpAme4yUa532P3vcJs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8cf63aa3-6ada-4a64-b48a-7a2fcee47862&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5328ab8e&sv=2)

In October 2024, CME Smart Money increased positions from 1,800 to 12,000 contracts, marking the largest holdings and addition of contracts in recorded data. Following this, BTC entered a one-sided rally, surpassing the $100K milestone.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FXoRkLxaUdoHBZ03WCglm%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De87bc198-ec1a-4e8d-862b-d1935c7ef28d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=14ff1fbf&sv=2)

* * *

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money#disclaimer)

# Cumberland USDT Distribution | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#waht-is-cumberland-usdt-distribution)

Waht is Cumberland USDT Distribution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FhanPI8mjXhM97cnjZhXF%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27d60db2-b740-488d-b283-8fc271dbed9f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=52f8e2ae&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#about-cumberland)

About Cumberland


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#company)

Company

*   Company: Cumberland DRW (“Cumberland”), the crypto trading division of DRW Holdings.
    
*   Parent: DRW is a Chicago-based proprietary trading firm founded in 1992.
    
*   Crypto Focus: Cumberland was launched in 2014 and is one of the earliest institutional players in the digital asset market.
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#core-businesses)

Core Businesses

*   OTC Trading – Facilitates large crypto transactions for institutions, miners, foundations, and family offices, minimizing slippage and market disruption.
    
*   Liquidity Provision – One of the largest liquidity providers in crypto, acting as a market maker across major exchanges such as Binance, OKX, and Coinbase.
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#why-track-cumberland)

Why Track Cumberland?

*   Key USDT Gateway: Cumberland is a primary partner of Tether Treasury, frequently handling newly minted USDT and distributing it to exchanges or institutional clients.
    
*   Not All Mints Equal: USDT issuance doesn’t always mean new inflows into crypto; some funds may be used for settlements, off-exchange transactions, or gray-market activity. CoinKarma monitors Cumberland’s wallets in real time to determine whether fresh USDT is actually entering exchanges and driving buy-side pressure.
    
*   Market Impact: Historical data shows that major USDT inflows via Cumberland—such as in early 2024, late 2024, and mid-2025—preceded strong market rallies, highlighting its influence on liquidity cycles.
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#how-to-use-cumberland-usdt-distribution)

How to Use Cumberland USDT Distribution


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A red box marks when Cumberland’s 7-day cumulative USDT transfers exceed $500M.
    
*   Logic: If a large USDT mint is quickly funneled to exchanges, it often fuels taker-buy demand over the next 1–2 weeks. After such an event, the effectiveness of LIQ red bars (bearish liquidity signals) tends to weaken, making premature shorts riskier.
    

**Case Review with Overall LIQ** On the daily chart, highlight candles at points where Cumberland’s 7-day inflows exceed $500M.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FWkWTQvGWzA3BuWB1S4rK%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db4ae628d-af6d-46d7-8e30-4fed2125b08c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c10ae440&sv=2)

On the hourly chart, compare these red-box periods with LIQ signals. Example: after significant inflows (points ① and ②), markets continued to rally despite LIQ red bars suggesting resistance.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FyAxl91Bsiv1JwJU4efnf%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8bee5bce-9555-4d86-9877-46aa0467eed1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=74b03a17&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#indicator-value)

Indicator Value


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   LIQ red bars: Reliable short signals during choppy or sideways markets.
    
*   Problem: In strong uptrends, they often trigger early shorts that get squeezed.
    
*   Solution: Combine LIQ with Cumberland USDT Distribution to filter signals. When large inflows support the market, fade LIQ shorts and avoid false bearish setups.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution#disclaimer)

# Short filter | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/short-filter#what-is-short-filter)

What is Short filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When the Market Pulse Index triggers a short signal and the Cumberland USDT Distribution’s 7-day cumulative USDT transfer volume exceeds 10% of overall liquidity (USD), the “No-Short Filter” is triggered.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/short-filter#how-to-use-short-filter)

How to use Short filter


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Short Filter (i.e., the “No-Short Filter”) is designed to keep you from shorting into a one-sided uptrend (the ❌ marks on the chart). While it may cause you to miss some short-side profits, it helps you avoid getting squeezed by shorting too early—such as at points A and B. In many cases, once the “No-Short Filter” fires, more attractive short setups tend to appear later (see the orange arrows).

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FglKphISdaBQU93aXeKPn%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7e192879-f574-44e9-9fe5-5a3cef63084b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=342172b8&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/short-filter#disclaimer)

# Volatility Term Structure | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#what-is-volatility-term-structure)

What is Volatility Term Structure


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The volatility term structure describes how at-the-money (ATM) implied volatility (IV) varies across option expiries (tenors). Put simply, it compares the relative levels of short-, mid-, and long-dated ATM IV to gauge how the market’s expectations for future volatility are shifting.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#normal-vs.-inverted-structures)

Normal vs. Inverted Structures

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#normal-upward-sloping)

Normal (upward-sloping):

*   Long-dated ATM IV > Short-dated ATM IV
    
*   Longer horizons embed more uncertainty, so the market usually assigns higher forward volatility to longer expiries.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#inverted-downward-sloping)

Inverted (downward-sloping):

*   Short-dated ATM IV > Long-dated ATM IV
    
*   An inversion signals the market expects outsized movement in the near term—often around periods of extreme sentiment (e.g., just before a crash or ahead of a bottoming reversal).
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#a-note-on-implied-volatility-iv)

A Note on Implied Volatility (IV)

In options markets, IV reflects the market’s expectation for the magnitude of future price moves in the underlying.

*   High IV → the market anticipates large moves; uncertainty is elevated.
    
*   Low IV → the market expects calmer conditions; uncertainty is subdued.
    

Among the various IV measures, ATM IV is watched most closely because it best captures the market’s “baseline” view of future volatility.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#how-to-use-the-volatility-term-structure)

How to Use the Volatility Term Structure

Practitioners typically compare ATM IV across three time frames:

*   Short term: 1-month ATM IV
    
*   Mid term: 3-month ATM IV
    
*   Long term: 6-month ATM IV
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#key-configurations)

Key Configurations

Setup

Context

Market Interpretation

Volatility Expectation

① 1M < 3M < 6M

Normal structure

The market is steady; long-term uncertainty is higher than short-term.

Volatility expected to be stable.

② 1M > 3M > 6M

Fully inverted

The market expects pronounced near-term turbulence.

Intense short-term volatility likely; often seen before crashes or ahead of bottom reversals.

③ 1M ≈ 3M ≈ 6M

Completely flat

The market lacks a clear directional view and is waiting for a catalyst.

Typically the calm before a volatility breakout.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#post-trade-backtest-takeaways)

Post-Trade / Backtest Takeaways

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FLqbqkVFkocVyQTJIRQBy%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b9c98be-a9ed-429c-9258-fa8a9534081c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7086c1ea&sv=2)

From the illustrative chart: when the orange line (1M ATM IV) rises above the blue and purple lines (3M and 6M ATM IV)—i.e., an inversion—the VTS panel highlights these periods in red. These episodes often line up with phases when the BTC market is about to experience pronounced volatility.

Typical behaviors observed:

*   Inversion during an uptrend → prone to reversal lower or transition into a choppy range.
    
*   Inversion during a downtrend → prone to reversal higher or transition into a consolidation range.
    

The yellow boxes mark inverted regimes where short-dated ATM IV spikes—often reflecting a jump in hedging demand—after which price frequently shows a clear directional change. When the inversion fades and the structure normalizes (1M ATM IV falls back below 3M/6M), realized volatility tends to decline and price action often compresses/mean-reverts.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#conclusion-limits-of-vts)

Conclusion: Limits of VTS

The volatility term structure is effective for tracking changes in volatility expectations, but it is not directional. An inversion indicates the market expects more near-term movement; it does not say whether price will rise or fall. In practice, traders pair VTS with other tools—e.g., sentiment gauges, liquidity metrics, or options skew—to cross-validate signals before acting.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

# USDC/USDT Premium | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usdc-usdt-premium#what-is-usdc-usdt-premium)

What is USDC/USDT Premium


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

USDC/USDT Premium measures the price spread between USDC and USDT. Although both are marketed as being pegged to USD at 1:1, in real trading their prices can trade at a premium or discount due to differences in demand and funding pressure. That spread can be used to infer short-term capital flows and where market pressure is coming from—and it tends to be highly correlated with BTC’s short-term price swings.

When there is no meaningful inflow of fresh external capital, the market is largely driven by internal capital rotation. Since USDT is the dominant settlement currency in crypto, its trading volume and depth have long exceeded those of USDC. As a result, BTC/USDT—rather than BTC/USDC—typically acts as the true benchmark for short-term price direction.

So when major players have an incentive to sell BTC in the short run, they usually start in the more liquid BTC/USDT market. This can lead to BTC/USDT trading below BTC/USDC, because BTC/USDT bears the brunt of the active selling pressure (and the opposite happens when they’re buying). Once that gap opens, an arbitrage opportunity emerges: arbitrageurs buy BTC where it’s cheaper (BTC/USDT), sell it where it’s more expensive (BTC/USDC), then sell the USDC they receive back into USDT to complete the loop. Therefore, when USDC/USDT Premium falls below 0, it often indicates that the dominant flow driving the market is net selling BTC.

Putting the logic together—using USDC/USDT Premium < 0 as an example:

1.  Large capital sells BTC on BTC/USDT → BTC/USDT leads the decline
    
2.  This creates BTC/USDT < BTC/USDC → arbitrage opportunities appear
    
3.  Arbitrage flows step in: buy BTC on cheaper BTC/USDT, sell BTC on richer BTC/USDC
    
4.  Arbitrageurs then sell the USDC proceeds back into USDT → pushing USDC/USDT Premium below 0
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usdc-usdt-premium#how-to-use-usdc-usdt-premium)

How to use USDC/USDT Premium


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Using USDC/USDT Premium < 0 as an example: in an environment with no incremental external capital, whenever the USDC/USDT Premium turns negative, the market often shows short-term topping behavior soon after.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FSeBgIXlGvi3rADvjPHD2%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6512139b-05f5-45c5-89ed-014055a397b1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aefbdb63&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/usdc-usdt-premium#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

# BTC 25Δ Skew | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#waht-is-btc-25d-skew)

Waht is BTC 25Δ Skew


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

25Δ Skew measures the difference in implied volatility (IV) between put and call options with the same delta magnitude (±0.25)：

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F4IIyZnPaJC0RgTkx8cAZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De5955f81-d2ee-4699-824a-dd6d1c5f45c0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=745c40c5&sv=2)

**Key terms**

*   IV (Implied Volatility): The market’s expectation of future price variability, embedded in option prices.
    
*   ATM (At-The-Money): The IV of options whose strike is closest to the current spot price; often used as a normalization anchor for comparing vol levels across maturities or strikes.
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#why-25d)

📘 Why “25Δ”?

“25Δ” denotes options with delta ≈ ±0.25—i.e., out-of-the-money (OTM) options a step away from spot.

*   25Δ Put: Slightly below spot; proxies demand for downside hedging.
    
*   25Δ Call: Slightly above spot; proxies willingness to pay for upside exposure.
    

Comparing the IV of these two strikes reveals the market’s directional bias and risk appetite.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#how-to-read-btc-25d-skew)

📊 How to Read BTC 25Δ Skew

Skew

Interpretation

Market Sentiment

\> 0

Put IV > Call IV

Fearful; hedging demand elevated (bearish bias)

< 0

Call IV > Put IV

Optimistic; strong appetite for upside/chasing rallies (bullish bias)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#extreme-sentiment-zones-1m-tenor-example)

Extreme sentiment zones（1M Tenor Example）

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F4k21Fc5XHbIxlmu6Wm4M%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8c12f0b-2352-41d5-8867-f0727186cd7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6c4601e6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#btc-25d-skew-practical-interpretation)

📈 BTC 25Δ Skew Practical Interpretation

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#skew-less-than-8-excessive-bullishness-call-enthusiasm-overheated)

Skew < −8 → Excessive bullishness (call enthusiasm overheated)

*   When call IV is materially higher than put IV, the market is broadly betting on upside.
    
*   In December 2024, BTC rallied sharply and the 25Δ skew dipped below −8 multiple times—an expression of exuberant sentiment. Such phases often carry elevated short-term risk and are prone to pullbacks.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#skew-greater-than-8-acute-fear-put-hedging-demand-surges)

Skew > +8 → Acute fear (put-hedging demand surges)

*   When put IV far exceeds call IV, hedging demand and fear dominate.
    
*   In early April 2025, skew printed above +8 repeatedly amid heightened macro headlines, reflecting a rush for protection. These episodes often coincide with sentiment “bottoms,” but price reversal still needs confirmation from structure/price action.
    

> Note： In crypto, extreme sentiment can persist. A skew below −8 does not imply an immediate top, and a skew above +8 does not guarantee an immediate bottom. Skew should complement—not replace—other signals.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#how-to-btc-25d-skew)

How to BTC 25Δ skew


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC 25Δ Skew is a sentiment gauge, not a standalone trading signal. It helps you:

*   Identify when fear/greed reaches extremes that often precede price turning points.
    
*   Contextualize risk: combine skew with price structure, breadth/liquidity metrics, funding/basis, and momentum to refine entries and exits.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#skew-iv-put-iv-call)

**Skew = IV(Put) − IV(Call)**

Skew > 0 (positive): Put IV > Call IV → crowd is paying up for downside protection → sentiment fearful.

*   Markets can rebound as panic becomes crowded, but wait for confirmation (e.g., momentum/market-structure turns).
    

Skew < 0 (negative): Call IV > Put IV → crowd is paying up for upside exposure → sentiment optimistic.

*   Markets can stall or mean-revert after excessive optimism; again, seek confirmation before acting.
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#how-to-read-btc-25d-skew-1)

How to Read BTC 25Δ Skew


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Skew

Interpretation

Extreme Threshold

Interpretation at Extreme

Skew > 0

Put IV > Call IV → market fear; bearish bias

Skew > 8

Extreme fear

Skew < 0

Call IV > Put IV → market optimism; bullish bias

Skew < -8

Extreme optimism

Time-Period (Tenor) Baseline: 1M

“Time Period” here refers to the option maturity used for comparison.

*   Very short-dated (e.g., 1-day): Hyper-sensitive to headlines; captures immediate fear/greed.
    
*   Long-dated (e.g., 1-year): Smoother; reflects expectations for the broader trend.
    
    Using 1-month as the baseline balances responsiveness with stability for most tactical reads.
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#btc-25d-skews-limitation)

BTC 25Δ skew's limitation


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC 25Δ Skew reflects market sentiment, not absolute buy/sell instructions. When skew reaches extremes, use it alongside other indicators (price action, liquidity, macro catalysts, positioning) to more reliably identify inflection points.

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#disclaimer)

**Disclaimer**

Thank you for using CoinKarma. The data provided is based on historical performance and cannot guarantee future market trends. The cryptocurrency market is highly volatile. Users must assess risks and bear responsibility for their decisions.

# Token Screener | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/token-screener#what-is-token-screener)

What is Token Screener?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Token Screener is an exclusive channel for members that provides hourly updates.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FkXRcbJANlh0KNXFdfps9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D88c31a48-497e-4ab8-9add-22ef61694b4b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5df70179&sv=2)

This channel categorizes all cryptocurrencies into four quadrants and uses color to indicate whether certain conditions are met. Coins that do not meet the criteria are shown in white, while BTC is always marked in orange on the quadrant chart.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FyJl1WOmmfzTEQaRBWY76%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74374c46-d34c-4d94-b7a3-e209e113b93f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ddff6b3a&sv=2)

Note 1: RSI\_Dif = the value obtained by subtracting BTC’s RSI from the coin’s RSI. A positive value indicates stronger relative strength; a negative value indicates weaker.

Note 2: LIQ Percentile = the percentile rank of the coin’s LIQ over the past month.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/token-screener#ru-he-yun-yong-token-screener)

How to Use Token Screener

Token Screener allows you to quickly identify strong tokens (Quadrant I) and weak tokens (Quadrant III). However, it’s essential not to rely solely on individual token data — you must also consider the overall market condition, primarily indicated by Bitcoin (referred to as BTC below).

In the crypto market, the price movements of altcoins remain highly correlated with BTC. Even if a specific altcoin shows strong individual metrics, if BTC is trending downward or broader market indicators are bearish, that altcoin will likely face headwinds and struggle to perform. This is mainly because many altcoins are traded against BTC (e.g., ALTs/BTC). So, even if an altcoin holds steady in USD terms, it can still perform poorly in BTC terms when BTC drops.

Therefore, when analyzing altcoins, it’s not enough to assess their standalone data — you must also evaluate BTC’s overall condition.

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/token-screener#ju-ti-cao-zuo)

How to Use It in Practice

1.  Use Token Screener to quickly identify strong and weak tokens.
    
2.  Observe BTC’s position on the Y-axis in the Token Screener chart:
    
    *   The higher BTC appears on the Y-axis, the stronger the bullish tokens on the chart tend to be.
        
    *   The lower BTC appears on the Y-axis, the stronger the bearish tokens on the chart tend to be.
        
    

● Case Studies: Identifying Strong and Weak Tokens

*   Strong Token (April 7, 2025 – 15:00) – $SUI
    

$SUI appeared in the strong token list on Token Screener. Custom Signal data indicated supportive market liquidity (green arrow). Following this signal, $SUI experienced an impressive rally, significantly outperforming $BTC.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F0iFFDYXyr5NxaOrpk4iO%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D95401981-3d36-45f4-94dc-564583aab8fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ce51f02b&sv=2)

*   Strong Token (April 7, 2025 – 15:00) – $DOGE
    

$DOGE also showed up in the strong token list, with Custom Signal confirming favorable liquidity conditions (green arrow). It subsequently posted a major price surge, far outpacing $BTC.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FlphSro81ASjmVUBzalgh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa0cfad1-4076-491e-b6ff-230667a403c9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fc150bff&sv=2)

*   Weak Token (March 3, 2025 – 02:00) – $SOL
    

$SOL was flagged as a weak token by Token Screener. Custom Signal showed negative market liquidity conditions (red arrow), and $SOL later underwent a sharp correction, dropping more than $BTC.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FGtlj1AaJdldSVkPH2dHZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6039f24e-7dec-4e5a-9492-377bde07d5a8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=859c7c2&sv=2)

*   Weak Token (March 3, 2025 – 02:00) – $LTC

# Market Pulse | English | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/market-pulse#what-is-market-pulse)

What is Market Pulse


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Market Pulse is an index ranging from 0 to 100, calculated based on 11 indicators from CoinKarma.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FgHbmwdABk3FysjgWKdxu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb6af46f-b3dd-4701-b02b-16286790d92b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9cbcf463&sv=2)

# USD/USDT Interest Rate | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate#shen-mo-shi-usdusdt-interest-rate)

什麼是USD/USDT Interest Rate


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

除了幣圈獨有的永續合約和資金費率外，幣圈依舊有傳統金融常見的借貸利率。借貸利率是中心化交易所上，進行現貨借貸行為所產生的利率。因此有兩個重點可以進行分析，第一個是中心化交易所，第二個就是利率高低。目前中心化交易所採取的依據為目前世界上最大的交易所 Binance 以及以借貸著名的老牌交易所 Bitfinex。

●Binance

目前身為世界上最大的交易所，因此裡面的會員組成會相對複雜，且散戶比例會相對較高， 這樣的特性可能導致在市場進入價值發現的階段或是牛市時，大家的行為會普遍比較激進。

●Bitfinex

Bitfinex身為歷史最悠久的交易所及其背景，交易成員有蠻大機率為幣圈原生主力(巨鯨)，因此透過觀察Bitfinex的借貸利率，可以判斷市場所謂的聰明錢是如何判斷當前市場行情。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate#ru-he-yun-yong-usdusdt-interest-rate)

如何運用USD/USDT Interest Rate


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

USD/USDT Interest Rate屬於一款週期性較大的指標。因兩家交易所的各自特性及成員組成，我們將Binance的借貸行為視為散戶、Bitfinex的借貸行為視為主力。

可以發現

*   當Bitfinex的借貸利率 > Binance的借貸利率，往往是行情底部，
    
*   當Bitfinex的借貸利率 < Binance的借貸利率，往往是行情頂部。
    

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousExchange App iOS Ranking](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/exchange-app-ios-ranking)
[NextBinance Insurance Fund](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund)

# CVD(Cumulative Volume Delta) | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#shen-mo-shi-cvdcumulative-volume-delta)

什麼是CVD(Cumulative Volume Delta)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

CVD是一種用來分析市場買賣力量平衡的指標，它累積了在一定時間內買入和賣出訂單的交易量差異。

簡言之，可以把CVD當作一段行情下「市價單」買賣力道的呈現。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#wei-shen-mo-coinkarma-yao-te-bie-shou-lu-cvd-zhi-biao)

為什麼Coinkarma要特別收錄CVD指標？


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

是因為LIQ的相關指標，皆是基於現貨訂單簿的買單 (bid) 以及賣單 (ask) 即「限價單」所組成，而當一段行情中，「市價單」的力量持續往某一方向推進時，就有可能同時消耗大多數的「限價單」，這會使LIQ相關數據呈現過度延伸。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta#ru-he-yun-yong-cvd)

如何運用 CVD


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

此段的介紹，我們將以LIQ過度延伸的部分去對比CVD，探討如何用CVD去過濾LIQ過度延伸的情況。

以下舉例：Overall LIQ紅柱時的過度延伸，黃框處頻繁出現Overall LIQ紅柱，但是價格卻屢創高點，同時我們觀察到CVD，可以發現這段的市價買盤非常猛烈，這使許多賣單 (ask)「限價單」被消耗，造成Overall LIQ過度延伸。因此可以透過觀察CVD去過濾掉開空的選擇。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdPatF0u0S-dyQKBnnSG0Cgmg24sX5SdKZ7fud8VuDQQshzfMRXMWvJAaNzcM6osxW4WPmiHVIC18niqpviBZGlEhaz6CrUm9LmPeLIFvNucab3W9Pb12lKmujhfbdtDmKZ9urQYA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=738accf0&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousBinance Insurance Fund](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund)
[NextCME Smart Money](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money)

# Future Basis Rolling APY | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#shen-mo-shi-future-basis-rolling-apy)

什麼是 Future Basis Rolling APY


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcjdPzxa-vK-CM3VEruaPpVI9-NE9zcrBooNsjF34QJccitTYW0ZLlke6_9nDdc3iSz9piHfEcow46WlEsj-Co3FGLTNX0U6o0oOhAnZrAAPVrYCgGOHn3tUm3sghHHF7hTHvlV%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b06f7c2d&sv=2)

遠期交割合約跟現貨價格的差距稱為基差，由於幣圈市場情緒長期看漲，大部分幣種的遠期交割合約都有正基差。這就出現了套利機會，假設 BTC 某個交割合約基差為 2%，距離交割還有 30天，那套利者就可以買進現貨並且做空等量的遠期交割合約來套取這 2% 的利差，這可以說是 free money，只要放到放到交割，這 2% 就是穩賺的。

以上述例子來說，換算的年化報酬率就是 2%\*(360/30)=24%，這稱為 Rolling APY，之所以是 Rolling （滾動），是因為這個報酬率會一直隨著交割時間越來越近而不斷改變，因為越接近交割日，遠期合約跟現貨的價差就會越收斂。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#ru-he-yun-yong-future-basis-rolling-apy)

如何運用 Future Basis Rolling APY


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

通常期貨市場越樂觀的時候， 市場大部分的人都會做多，這會造成遠期交割合約相對現貨的溢價擴大，Rolling APY 也會隨之上升，所以 Future Basis Rolling APY 跟資金費率(Funding Rate)一樣，可以用來衡量市場情緒。

從過去歷史來看，BTC 最近一個季度合約的 Rolling APY 有著以下意義：

*   0 以下 = 世界末日（2020/3/12大跌期間有出現過）
    
*   0-5% = 極度恐慌
    
*   5%-10% = 市場冷靜
    
*   10%-15% = 市場微熱
    
*   15%-20% = 市場狂熱
    
*   20%以上 = FOMO
    

預設值為（5, 20），用戶可自行透過覆盤調整參數。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#jie-yu-future-basis-rolling-apy-de-ju-xian-xing)

結語-Future Basis Rolling APY 的侷限性


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如同資金費率(Funding Rate)一樣，以往 BTC 現貨 ETF 還沒通過的時候，正規基金要取得 BTC 的曝險相對困難，現在買 ETF 做空合約非常方便，這會壓低了合約跟現貨的價差使數據有所鈍化。因此使用 Rolling APY 判斷市場情緒時，可能需要降低標準，以往 20% 以上屬 FOMO，現階段 Rolling APY 達 15%-20% 可能已經屬於 FOMO 情況。

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousALT Resilient Index](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index)
[NextOI-Weighted Funding Rate](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate)

Last updated 11 months ago

*   [如何運用 Future Basis Rolling APY](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#ru-he-yun-yong-future-basis-rolling-apy)
    
*   [結語-Future Basis Rolling APY 的侷限性](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy#jie-yu-future-basis-rolling-apy-de-ju-xian-xing)

# OI-Weighted Funding Rate | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#shen-mo-shi-oiweighted-funding-rate-chi-cang-jia-quan-zi-jin-feil)

什麼是 OI-Weighted Funding Rate (持倉加權資金費率)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

以下以 BTC OI-Weighted Funding Rate 為例

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcfRoNOwoVujyky-uXV_wJQD5FgElARc-CZeuO1OzlvpMlD_LhzJaqT7GBXJs_1Exn8uxqAJzjAG6l5uCmveKdJtJcKFrm79kJ5aiHAjzG-LNLrb32mT2DuUmXfJkuRUpmImWpxWw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28b575e0&sv=2)

資金費率（Funding rates）是加密貨幣交易所為了保持永續合約價格與標的資產價格之間的平衡而設定的費率。資金費率一般都會是常數(0.01%)，而當溢價高到一定水平，資金費率就會開始調升，由於做多成本提高，這會促使多頭平倉，把永續合約價格壓下來；相反地，如果永續合約低於現貨價格太多，資金費率也會開始由正轉負，這會促使空頭平空，把永續合約價格拉回正常水位。

資金費率由利率以及溢價控制，因此針對溢價去理解資金費率的變化條件：

溢價指數( P) = \[Max(0,衝擊買方出價-價格指數) – Max(0,價格指數-衝擊賣方出價)\] / 價格指數

而持倉加權資金費率（OI-Weighted Funding Rate）是依各大交易所的BTC永續合約持倉進行加權計算。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#ru-he-yun-yong-oiweighted-funding-rate)

如何運用 OI-Weighted Funding Rate


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

當合約市場趨於樂觀的時候， 市場槓桿做多的情緒旺盛，這會造成永續合約相對現貨的溢價擴大，資金費率(Funding Rate)也會隨之上升

所以 OI-Weighted Funding Rate 跟 Future Basis Rolling APY 一樣，可以用來衡量市場情緒。

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#zi-jin-feilbiao-sheng-de-zhuang-kuang-yi-wei-zhu-yong-xu-he-yue-jia-ge-gao-wu-xian-huo-jia-ge-hen-du)

● 資金費率飆升的狀況（意味著永續合約價格高於現貨價格很多），有可能的情況會是：

1\. 價格處於上漲趨勢，多頭激情開倉，且槓桿較大，拉高了永續合約價格

2\. 價格處於下降趨勢，多頭激進抄底，逆勢扛單，導致永續合約價格相對偏高

無論是哪一個狀況，其實都對多頭較為不利：

1\. 代表市場情緒樂觀，且相較空頭，多頭槓桿倍數較高，更有可能是散戶陣營在開多，更容易翻車

2\. 代表可能有相當規模的多頭倉位即將面臨爆倉或止損的命運，空方佔優

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#zi-jin-feilxia-jiang-de-zhuang-kuang-yi-wei-zhu-yong-xu-he-yue-jia-ge-di-wu-xian-huo-jia-ge-hen-duo)

● 資金費率下降的狀況（意味著永續合約價格低於現貨價格很多），有可能的情況會是：

1\. 價格處於下跌趨勢，空頭激情開倉，且槓桿較大，拉低了永續合約價格

2\. 價格處於上漲趨勢，空頭激進開空，逆勢扛單，導致永續合約價格相對偏低

無論是哪一個狀況，其實都對空頭較為不利：

1\. 代表市場情緒悲觀，且相較多頭，空頭槓桿倍數較高，更有可能是散戶陣營在開空，更容易翻車

2\. 代表可能有相當規模的空頭倉位即將面臨爆倉或止損的命運，多方佔優

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#jie-yu-oiweighted-funding-rate-de-ju-xian-xing)

結語-OI-Weighted Funding Rate 的侷限性


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

如同 Future Basis Rolling APY 一樣，以往 BTC 現貨 ETF 還沒通過的時候，正規基金要取得 BTC 的曝險相對困難，現在買 ETF 做空合約非常方便，大量傳統機構入場套利會使資金費率數據有所鈍化。因此現在使用 OI-Weighted Funding Rate 判斷市場情緒時，相較前幾輪週期，基準需要往下移動。

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousFuture Basis Rolling APY](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy)
[NextBitfinex Indicators](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/bitfinex-indicators)

*   [如何運用 OI-Weighted Funding Rate](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#ru-he-yun-yong-oiweighted-funding-rate)
    
*   [● 資金費率飆升的狀況（意味著永續合約價格高於現貨價格很多），有可能的情況會是：](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/oi-weighted-funding-rate#zi-jin-feilbiao-sheng-de-zhuang-kuang-yi-wei-zhu-yong-xu-he-yue-jia-ge-gao-wu-xian-huo-jia-ge-hen-du)

# Exchange App iOS Ranking | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/exchange-app-ios-ranking#shen-mo-shi-exchange-app-ios-ranking)

什麼是Exchange App iOS Ranking


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

iOS App Ranking 是在美國地區中心化交易所的下載量排名。

通常在市場冷清的時候，許多人都漸漸淡出市場，導致關注市場的注意力降低。 但當市場進入情緒瘋狂的時候，看到許多人賺錢的消息，會使人們趨之若鶩的進入市場，就連擦鞋的小孩都會想找門路進入市場，這就是俗稱的「擦鞋童效應」。

因此透過觀察 Coinbase App 的下載量排名，可以判斷是否有擦鞋童效應的產生，當下載排名進入前幾名時，象徵市場已經非常瘋狂，大家都想找方法進入市場，反之亦然。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/exchange-app-ios-ranking#ru-he-yun-yong-exchange-app-ios-ranking)

如何運用Exchange App iOS Ranking


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

指標的藍線數值為 Coinbase 在美國地區的財經類 APP 熱度排名，因此數值越低代表排名越靠前。當 Coinbase App 排名越高，代表目前美國市場散戶對 Crypto 的 mind share 越高。當排名衝進 Top 10，超越了一些傳統財經類 APP（如盈透證券、Yahoo Finance 等）時，代表行情短線可能過熱，該進場的散戶都進場了。

復盤過往牛市，當 Coinbase 排名長時間都在 Top 10 時，有較高機率為階段性行情的頂部，當排名在高位持續越久，越有機會成為 Global top。下圖以前 10 名作為一個基準，復盤 2021 與 2024 牛市供讀者參考。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeNaY__G6Tp_2IKkxrijn-vOyVJd9uL_nV9H2aZvjtyjDYXNyaE3Xn5sCFOPkoM54Rtn9QxYoDlvUm31J0Ny7mxEXvFqKUllafXDDp27ewTKwqskFetlaq4eq9KnMHvqEJMuYpx9w%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=834d2fd1&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousKarma Index](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/karma-index)
[NextUSD/USDT Interest Rate](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/usd-usdt-interest-rate)

# Ultron Signal | English | CoinKarma

What is Ultron Signal?

Ultron Signal is an exclusive copy trading strategy available to Gold members.

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252FYyQroRHRIEnTdkiTdCKR%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc19d4c0d-4612-4304-9612-97d81c1a43b6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b9508c8&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/ultron-signal#how-to-subscribe-to-ultron-signal)

How to Subscribe to Ultron Signal


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ultron Signal currently offers two copy trading solutions:

1.  OKX Signal Trading Edition
    
2.  Hyperliquid Vault Edition
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3881674611-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FLNdPzU6psKxnGpgv182e%252Fuploads%252F4TxBdnTdLAixVtoDAqZt%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd1cfc54b-8439-4349-a518-283fbbba70b4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3b1bbdf6&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/ultron-signal#strategy-overview)

Strategy Overview

**Core Framework** Ultron Signal is powered by the proprietary **Market Pulse Index (MPI)**, which serves as the core indicator for assessing market strength, determining entry and exit points, and dynamically adjusting position size.

**Multi-Layer Dynamic Adjustment** The strategy integrates multiple market factors, including:

*   Long-term moving averages (trend direction)
    
*   RSI (market momentum)
    
*   Recent realized volatility (market activity)
    

These elements collectively influence the system’s threshold levels, allowing Ultron Signal to automatically adapt to changing market structures.

**No-Short Filter** When buy-side strength significantly outweighs sell pressure, the system activates a **“No-Short” protection mode**, temporarily disabling short positions to reduce counter-trend risks and enhance decision flexibility.

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/english/features-guide/ultron-signal#stop-loss-mechanism)

Stop-Loss Mechanism


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Ultron Signal does not employ a fixed stop-loss level.

The main reason is that each user applies different leverage, and a uniform stop-loss threshold could lead to delayed liquidation for high-leverage users or premature exits for low-leverage users. Instead, the strategy incorporates a **dynamic risk control framework**.

For example, when the strategy holds a long position and the market experiences an **overextended decline** while the **MPI starts to flatten out**, Ultron will automatically scale down or close positions _as the market rebounds_, creating a natural stop-loss effect.

Using **3× leverage** as an example: even during sharp drawdowns such as in **April 2025**, the **maximum drawdown (MDD)** was limited to around **20%**, keeping the risk within a controllable range. Therefore, we recommend operating the strategy with **leverage up to 3×**.

For users employing higher leverage, additional **take-profit and stop-loss conditions** can be customized within the **Advanced Settings** panel when subscribing to the OKX signal.

# ALT Resilient Index | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#shen-mo-shi-ari-zhi-biao-alt-resilient-index)

什麼是 ARI 指標(ALT Resilient Index)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXerpg0QZQSg9Jn-Zv3k3hg4QnpYdC2imQH9VZ1oIQyCRACN-gnfhDZbdf8IdUw_7rEAoiny_KtdHcrosbmp5FaJjH4lfMpZ7XWNW7MDfQszgdC_ht8gxGGmSxwA4uqjym3vy5J7Kg%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6dc6530a&sv=2)

在幣圈我們知道一個現象，當 BTC 大跌而山寨幣不跟跌時，通常是短線上一個相對安全的進場邊際，其基礎邏輯是， 當 BTC 下跌時，山寨幣往往會遭到更嚴重的拋售，當行情觸底，山寨幣的造市商會開始回收砸出去的籌碼，此時就會出現 ALT/BTC 匯率反彈的狀況，表現在價格上就是山寨下跌得比 BTC 更少，甚至逆勢反彈。

因此透過 ARI 指標可以在 BTC 大跌時，觀察山寨幣造市商對當前極端行情的判斷； 當 ARI 指標數值越高時，代表山寨幣的造市商願意承接市場拋壓的力量越大，換言之，就是造市商願意花真金白銀去護盤，這通常會是行情的止跌點。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#ru-he-yun-yong-ari-zhi-biao)

如何運用 ARI 指標


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

牛市通常不會是單邊一路漲到尾，而是中間伴隨著 BTC 單邊 10%-20% 以上的跌幅修正； 當行情修正發生時，透過 ARI 指標可以找出安全邊際高的進場位置。

● 單以 ARI 指標作為行情介入點

以下舉例這輪牛市中，BTC 比較大的單邊跌幅去對比 ARI 指標

◦ A 點：BTC ETF sell the news 事件

◦ B 點：以色列—哈瑪斯戰爭加劇

◦ C 點：日本央行提高基準利率，引發金融市場崩盤，加劇全球市場動盪

這些點位都是受外部因素影響且場內情緒較恐慌的位置，事後單看 ARI 指標都給出了相對低位的進場點。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeI_XXa4usjytO8bSE2_XJMFxaP0WH3EMNwJFFlA9sxph-2sx8-5XwYRKtvDJqEI4F9-xzLxI0eFmwvvsyx1H0MKEucaSicDwkZuxtyQFBmaIE1Bmy0l2Fdhrz9JT1jS8z11t_frQ%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5cf4a13&sv=2)

● 將 ARI 作為 LIQ 相關指標進場策略的濾網

以下舉例日本央行升息事件：

在日本央行 7 月 31 日貨幣無預警升息後，BTC 快速從 67K 跌至 58K 時 LIQ 給出了進場訊號(黃框)，但隨後再次下跌至最低 49K ，若此次我們加上 ARI 指標作為 LIQ 進場的過濾(橘框)，進場的安全邊際會提升非常多。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeDLQLgY54Qb7tg1K9Ap_8YtSfkoG4qC1ybuHDwHKMZB0CG3RJ8FxVAfSd8K13Z0A59uY5dGdpALZSEaFwNvHe-FirOoR2hHqb_01C5qgOntnTl3T5YfCwQHSv9_6NLrrGbch7nNg%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6d271edd&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/alt-resilient-index#jie-yu-arialt-resilient-index-zhi-biao-de-shi-yong-chang-jing-ji-qi-ju-xian-xing)

結語-ARI(ALT Resilient Index)指標的適用場景及其侷限性


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

● ARI 指標的適用場景

當行情發生大幅度修正時，即可透過 ARI 指標找出安全邊際高的進場位置。

● ARI 指標的侷限性

◦ 介入行情的交易機會少：ARI benchmark 設定為3，若單以 ARI 指標作為進場策略，觸發交易的交易機會會相對較少，用戶可以搭配其他指標達到其最大效用。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXePnmVCINOw16K2fUD_8M1hAFYx4p7tiuZ1ee29T9MyFhihq2F22rkXZyvjN5UxmI3_tmhArbMcn6XDoN4I5_6UToprhP0Oe5jAroV_qCeLxv-YBDJD6oCcyhr4-upnBhKYKLR99Q%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b9d6896c&sv=2)

◦ 無法 100% 標示絕對的低點：當觸發 ARI 指標時，代表造市商願意在此位階承接市場拋壓，但驅動行情的因素很多，當市場某些因素產生的拋壓大於造市商承接的力量時，價格還是有可能繼續探底。 以下舉例：2024/1 BTC sell the news 事件，當觸發 ARI 指標時，BTC 還是向下跌超10%，但事後看仍是一個不錯的進場位置。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeBH15Pd0IgR3R1-FNe8ciYtNvS30XEunhFhxviIvCgs5GOmmwLYEJMzkwoX1Ntp2GG0eY4CWJOMiiIG_ZOnIC5YP_KGRne1fMCnUtJtr1YLTeF0PIorC8jTVYQ0cELzYwCrPoFQw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=983dc8cb&sv=2)

**使用須知** 感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousLIQ](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/liq)
[NextFuture Basis Rolling APY](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/future-basis-rolling-apy)

Last updated 11 months ago

# Stablecoin Supply | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#shen-mo-shi-stablecoin-supply)

什麼是Stablecoin Supply


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Stablecoin Supply 是穩定幣 USDT、USDC 的流通市值指標。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#ru-he-yun-yong-stablecoin-supply)

如何運用 Stablecoin Supply


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#yi-shi-zhi-zui-da-de-wen-ding-bi-usdt-dui-bi-btc-jia-ge)

以市值最大的穩定幣-USDT對比BTC價格：

*   可以發現在2022年隨著市場下跌，USDT市值也隨之下降 → 資金流出市場，可以預期市場流動性不斷減少
    
*   而隨著2023-2024年市場開始復甦，USDT市值也隨之上升 → 資金流入市場，可以預期市場流動性不斷增加。
    

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXepJcCldLtoXiLwYqWpgsHegk4GW8g8aOKrtbLG33-nECvw7hOmtAr7rvxaWte5eQgfGvj6F24u2QGWIsTRexG5rSoiPHudrcm0L7tEIZ3EB7n-6dLzQB7ccXa644mIuaiP9waysQ%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=58c566fb&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply#zhong-dian-guan-cha-usdc-ni-shi-zeng-fa)

重點觀察：USDC逆勢增發

透過復盤發現，USDC 在短線上若出現與價格背離、逆勢增發現象，可能會形成底部。以下舉例：Overall LIQ出現綠柱+USDC增發超10億美金的情況，往往會形成短線上的區間底部。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcsbvGJaYjL1JXDvyGe3A_GlDis_J6rI5p3FzDDx8DnHHRaSG0kEQT6sodHXPb6P0gniZtYqSDWkadxBMw9F37H1OBggdhaB3m5qnTu6awt2LicaszU67YKN-AYci-f6njXwvj9hA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8baf7e54&sv=2)

# BTC ETF Net Flow | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#shen-mo-shi-btc-etf-net-flow)

什麼是BTC ETF Net Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC ETF Net Flow 是美股 BTC ETF 的淨流入(出)，CoinKarma 收錄了10支美股 BTC ETF 每日淨流入(出)的數據。

而 CoinKarma 之所以收錄 BTC ETF Net Flow，是因為透過復盤發現， 從 BTC ETF 流入的資金有一部分是套利倉位，對行情影響並不大，與我們直覺上認為 BTC ETF 的淨流入是看漲後市、淨流出是看跌後市的想法，有所不同，我們可以根據 BTC ETF 流入資金的狀況，來判斷期貨市場的情緒。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow#ru-he-yun-yong-btc-etf-net-flow)

如何運用 BTC ETF Net Flow


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

以下分析，美股投資人如何透過美股BTC ETF來進行套利：

*   當市場情緒好(過熱)，期貨溢價變高 --> 套利資金買進 BTC ETF，做空 CME 的期貨
    
*   當市場情緒差(恐慌)，期貨溢價變低 --> 套利資金賣出 BTC ETF，平倉 CME 的空單
    

所以當每次 BTC 行情到頂的時候， CME 的持倉量都會急遽拉升（對應的是 hedge fund 的 net short position 上升），行情下殺完之後，CME 持倉量也跟著下滑。

這批套利資金無需等到期貨交割才平倉，只要在幣圈市場情緒不斷發散跟收斂的過程中，一直在市場 fomo 時做空，市場恐慌時平空就可以賺錢。

透過觀察，IBIT 因為投資人屬性及手續費優勢，套利資金比較青睞 IBIT，其他 ETF 也有類似的套利行為，但規模遠不及 IBIT。因此我們夠過 IBIT 資金的流入流出狀況對比 BTC 價格，可以發現當 IBIT 資金淨流出或停止流入時（套利空單平倉、賣出 ETF 持倉），幾乎都是短期底部。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXewZR2WlR7nv3xj-K8BYGorHjvGApk0WlUdA_mQcBxrg-jyvIvgZc34Jcqd7ptrtrEUyqxQXOiT87vn2XmSUviUIlL9ZhykWJCsxGDAujKCASIBwqk-XZNqSVhRXUW9AvlOHPqvUg%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=125cccab&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousCME Smart Money](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money)
[NextStablecoin Supply](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply)

# Binance Insurance Fund | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#shen-mo-shi-binance-insurance-fund-he-yue-feng-xian-bao-zhang-ji-jin)

什麼是Binance Insurance Fund(合約風險保障基金)


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

根據 Binance 的介紹文檔所述：

*   數據解釋：合約風險保障基金是用於限制交易對手強平影響的安全機制，這能保護交易者免受破產倉位所生的不利損失，並有助於確保獲利倉位的收益全額支付予獲利的交易者。
    
*   基金來源：當倉位遭到強平時，除非該倉位在強平後屬於破產倉位，否則會在扣除用於維持倉位所需的部分資產後，作為強平清算手續費支付給幣安，而此手續費部分分配予合約風險保障基金。
    

綜上，我們知道永續合約是一個零和市場，有人賺錢就會有人賠錢，而在極端行情下，賠錢的一方的保證金無法足額支付給獲利的一方時，就會由合約風險保障基金來支付，因此在極端清算槓桿的行情之後，合約風險保障基金才會下降。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/binance-insurance-fund#ru-he-yun-yong-binance-insurance-fund)

如何運用Binance Insurance Fund


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Binance Insurance Fund 長期向上增長，當遇到巨量清算、導致用戶穿倉的行情，才可能使 Insurance Fund 減少，因此當 Binance Insurance Fund 減少時，我們可以判斷短線上已經過度清算，尤其當清算槓桿多頭時，對比此數據特別有奇效，通常會是階段底部。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXdMe81zmZrN2bueuxc3CCBTA-cZSI229r9i2CfC7OEUSIHhR3yZmbPleMAUT9V9UmVB04I9SnE9rRYhrQJWPwnfgJmPR3QKk-gDdtkofRmcWnwu9zfPi2dO32gJ5cUz7ELEMhSCrQ%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=311c8c84&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

# LSUR Z Index | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/lsur-z-index#shen-mo-shi-lsurzindex)

什麼是 LSUR Z Index


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LSUR Z index 是頭部幣種 OI 加權的 LSUR，跟過去 14 天平均值差距幾個標準差，舉例：-2 就是小於 2 個標準差。( 註：LSUR 是永續合約數據中，持倉人數多空比 ) 　

過去，在加密貨幣市場中，當 LSUR 小於 1，代表市場上做空的人多於做多的人，通常反映市場情緒過度悲觀，是價格可能觸底反彈的訊號，因此常被視為短期低點的參考指標。然而，這樣的邏輯在近年已逐漸失效，甚至出現反向變化 —— LSUR 小於 1 時，反而成為短期高點的前兆；至於真正的原因為何不得而知，CoinKarma 猜測，背後的關鍵原因之一，是機構資金的大量進場與對沖策略改變了市場結構。機構投資者與散戶不同，他們在現貨市場持有大量資產時，往往會在期貨市場建立空單進行風險對沖，並非單純看空市場。這使得市場在 LSUR 小於 1 的情況下，並不一定是情緒極度悲觀，而可能只是資金管理與策略性布局的結果。

即使市場結構發生改變，LSUR 仍然具有參考價值，透過 CoinKarma 的獨家算法，依然可以用於判斷市場短期多空可能的方向。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/lsur-z-index#ru-he-yun-yong-lsurzindex)

如何運用 LSUR Z Index


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

LSUR Z index 需搭配 CoinKarma 其他指標一起閱讀，以下舉例：

● 搭配 Overall LIQ 加以判斷市場可能的反轉點

在震盪行情中，當 LSUR Z index 與 Overall LIQ 共振時，找出潛在的行情反轉點。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeiUAmf97NCa1gCl_ACrqQpjjK7oAA1erinkCVILwnsmJEdZAQNSsoXdXaU6pAz_CkNZghr-_TZuS66-QM7c-L3KvJBYQa86A9lxLMh49GrXLz8SEoCwf9xIGzrm1wamx8fxx0kPw%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd27ac76&sv=2)

● 判斷 LIQ 相關指標與 LSUR Z index 可能過度延伸的警訊 黃框：當 LIQ 相關指標與 LSUR Z index 都出現行情可能回調的情況下，但價格仍然保持強勢，說明此處震盪趨勢中的有效因子正在鈍化，應避免做空。 ( 行情可能正由震盪趨勢轉為單邊趨勢 )

紫框：當 LSUR Z index 出現小於 -2 值時，搭配 LIQ 相關指標可以過濾其訊息，避免單就 LSUR Z index 做空。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXeXR3hDJmv7QVoxYa_QSB-qZotxhDFoC9k7WMFXVgMu-dHelxpun4lUFYbGQKlKE5PSZj-WofTz3tkOl-2I8SrnrpHx8ktIAdu6u2DevrfX4OKZhyrR_JWMST6_nnjfd2e2awBq%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1e51eca4&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousStablecoin Supply](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/stablecoin-supply)
[NextCumberland USDT Distribution](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cumberland-usdt-distribution)

# Short Filter | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/short-filter#shen-mo-shi-short-filter)

什麼是 Short filter


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

當 Market Pulse Index 達做空值時，但 Cumberland USDT Distribution 近 7 天 USDT 累積轉帳量超過 10% overall liquidity( in USD )，會觸發「No-Short Filter」。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/short-filter#ru-he-yun-yong-short-filter)

如何運用 Short filter


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Short Filter 是為了避免在單邊上漲行情中去做空的濾網指標( 如圖中 ❌ 處 )，可能會錯失一些做空的盈利機會，但能有效避免如圖中 A 點、B 點，過早做空而被嘎空的情況，而往往在觸發「No-Short Filter」後，後續仍有較佳的做空機會( 如圖中橘色箭頭處 )。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252Ff2SVcpHC4K3zOWie5ML9%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc3aa129a-7246-4225-9860-b8d20bb25198&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e361ad5c&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

# USDC/USDT Premium | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/usdc-usdt-premium#shen-mo-shi-usdcusdt-premium)

什麼是 USDC/USDT Premium


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

USDC/USDT Premium 是衡量 USDC 相對於 USDT 價差的指標。雖然兩者都標榜與1美元掛鉤，但在實際交易中，價格會因市場需求差異與資金壓力出現折溢價，而兩者的價差關係，可用來判斷短線資金的流向與市場承壓方向，其與 BTC 的短期價格波動具有高度相關性。

在沒有外部增量資金進入的情況下，市場主要由場內既有資金循環，而 USDT 是加密貨幣整體市場的主要結算單位，其交易量與深度長期佔比都是遠超過 USDC 的，因此 BTC/USDT 相較 BTC/USDC ，前者才是短線真正決定價格方向的基準價格。

所以，當主力在短線上有誘因要賣出 BTC 時，會從流動性較高的 BTC/USDT 開始，這會造成 BTC/USDT< BTC/USDC 的現象 ，因前者主動承壓(買入則相反)，此時套利空間也隨之出現，套利資金會在 BTC/USDT 買入價格較低的 BTC，在 BTC/USDC 賣出價格較高的 BTC，再將獲取的 USDC 拋售換回 USDT，完成套利，所以當 USDC/USDT Premium 低於 0 時，通常代表驅動市場的主要資金正在賣出 BTC。 綜合以上的邏輯整理，以 USDC/USDT Premium < 0 為例：

1.  大資金在 BTC/USDT 拋售 → BTC/USDT 價格領跌
    
2.  造成 BTC/USDT < BTC/USDC 的現象 → 出現套利機會
    
3.  套利資金介入－在價格較低的 BTC/USDT 購買 BTC，並於價格較貴的 BTC/USDC 出售 BTC
    
4.  套利者最後將獲取的 USDC 拋售回 USDT → 導致 USDC/USDT < 0
    

因此 USDC/USDT Premium < 0 通常代表市場大資金在賣 BTC。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/usdc-usdt-premium#ru-he-yun-yong-usdcusdt-premium)

如何運用 USDC/USDT Premium


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

以 USDC/USDT Premium < 0 舉例，在沒有外部增量資金進入的情況下，每當 USDC/USDT Premium 轉負時，通常短線上會出現觸頂現象。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FP0kdOC4XTT5vgUO4RF9O%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6199912-9e7c-4c5c-829e-44f9b05e6ae8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2186e167&sv=2)

**使用須知** 感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousShort Filter](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/short-filter)

# BTC 25Δ skew | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#shen-mo-shi-btc-25-skew)

什麼是 BTC 25Δ skew


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

25Δ Skew 反映市場對於看跌期權（Put）與看漲期權（Call）在相同 Delta 條件下的隱含波動率差異：

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FnPKa5VNxwanqtAKLkcJZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6383ae2-a531-45d7-ad43-e7856368cc42&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=333373db&sv=2)

其中：

*   IV（Implied Volatility）：期權價格反映的市場預期波動。
    
*   ATM（At-The-Money）：平值期權的隱含波動率，用於標準化比較。
    

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#wei-shen-mo-yong-25)

📘 為什麼用 25Δ

「25Δ」代表期權的 Delta 約為 ±0.25， 即距離現價一段距離的「虛值期權」(Out-of-the-money)。

*   25Δ Put：距現價略低，反映市場對「下跌避險需求」。
    
*   25Δ Call：距現價略高，反映市場對「上漲押注意願」。
    

透過比較這兩者的 IV，可以觀察市場對未來漲跌方向的偏好。

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#ru-he-jie-du-btc-25-skew)

📊 如何解讀 BTC 25Δ Skew

Skew 值

意涵

市場情緒

\> 0

Put IV > Call IV

市場恐懼、避險需求強（偏空）

< 0

Call IV > Put IV

市場樂觀、追漲意願強（偏多）

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#ji-duan-qing-xu-qu-jian-yi-1m-qi-quan-wei-li)

極端情緒區間（以 1M 期權為例）

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1729336661-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FJw2jrjZQmACHsCUyfYLT%252Fuploads%252FxVoE3G10GFRBpARwntqj%252Funknown.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4438002e-00f1-40bb-b49e-02bba517ed8f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be3780fc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#btc-25-skew-shi-zhan-jie-du)

📈 BTC 25Δ Skew 實戰解讀

**Skew < -8 → 市場極度樂觀（Call 看漲情緒過熱）**

*   當 Call 隱含波動率顯著高於 Put，代表市場普遍押注上漲。 在上圖中可見 2024 年 12 月，BTC 在短期內大幅拉升，Skew 多次低於 -8，顯示市場情緒亢奮。
    
*   通常此階段為短線風險偏高區，情緒過熱後容易出現回調。
    

**Skew > +8 → 市場極度恐懼（Put 避險需求強烈）**

*   當 Put 隱含波動率遠高於 Call，代表市場集中避險、恐懼升溫。 在上圖中可見 2025 年 4 月初（川普撤稅消息階段），Skew 多次高於 +8，市場避險需求急升。
    
*   這類時期常是短線情緒底部區，但需結合價格結構確認反轉。
    

備註：Crypto 市場的情緒極端可長時間延續：

樂觀階段 Skew 維持低於 -8 並不一定立即反轉，反之亦然。因此，Skew 不應單獨作為交易訊號，而應用來輔助判斷整體市場情緒溫度。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#ru-he-yun-yong-btc-25-skew)

如何運用 BTC 25Δ skew


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC 25Δ Skew 能夠反映市場對未來的樂觀預期或避險需求，是判斷市場情緒的重要輔助指標。

當市場恐懼或貪婪至一定程度時，Skew 的變化往往先於價格出現轉折。

#### 

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#skew-iv-put-iv-call)

**Skew = IV(Put) − IV(Call)**

• Skew 為正：多數人買入 Put 避險，Put 價格較貴 → 市場情緒較恐懼

Skew 為正時，代表多數人正在買入 Put 避險，看跌情緒高漲，然而，市場常因為恐慌情緒過度集中，價格反而容易出現反彈或築底。

• Skew 為負：多數人買入 Call 押漲，Call 價格較貴 → 市場情緒較樂觀

Skew 為負時，代表多數人正在買入 Call 押漲，看漲情緒高漲，然而，市場常因為市場過於樂觀，價格往往形成區間頂部或出現回調。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#zong-jie-btc-25-skew-de-yun-yong-shuo-ming)

總結 BTC 25Δ Skew 的運用說明


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Skew 值

意涵

極端閾值

意涵

Skew > 0

Put 較高，整體市場恐懼看跌

Skew > 8

市場極度恐懼

Skew < 0

Call 較高，整體市場樂觀看漲

Skew < -8

市場極度樂觀

Time Period 基準設定為 = 1M → Time Period 是「觀察期權期限結構的跨度」—— 也就是拿多短期的期權或多長期的期權來比較。

舉例：

*   1 天期的期權（超短） → 對突發事件極度敏感，反映「立即恐懼或貪婪」。
    
*   1 年期的期權（長期） → 反映市場對長期趨勢的穩定預期。
    

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-25d-skew#jie-yu-btc-25-skew-de-ju-xian-xing)

結語 - BTC 25Δ skew 的侷限性


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

BTC 25Δ skew 反映的是「市場情緒」，而非絕對的買賣信號，當 Skew 出現極端值時，結合其他指標相互搭配，能更準確抓住市場的行情拐點。

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[NextVolatility Term Structure](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/volatility-term-structure)

# CME Smart Money | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money#shen-mo-shi-cme-smart-money)

什麼是CME Smart Money


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

在市場上有一些巨鯨，他們的持倉能有一定的程度影響市場，因為當他們願意買進時，就會為市場帶來買方的支撐力道。除此之外，信息落差一直都是在市場上賺錢的根本之一，觀察有機會具備信息落差的鯨魚，就有機會為我們分辨出市場後續可能的趨勢。

在2024年BTC ETF通過的前後，市場都圍繞在此敘事，而當時最方便美國傳統金融交易的交易者交易BTC的地方便是芝加哥期貨交易所 (CME)。

CME Smart Money 是透過篩選在 CME 不同種類的交易員，去選出持倉變化在走勢上有 alpha 的那組人，歸集成的指標。

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cme-smart-money#ru-he-yun-yong-cme-smart-money)

如何運用 CME Smart Money


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   單位：張；一張5顆BTC。
    
*   讀取：０軸以上為淨多頭；0軸以下為淨空頭
    
*   更新時間：數據更新週期為台北（UTC+8)星期六更新當周星期二的倉位狀況。
    

2022-2023年每當 CME Smart money 轉 net short 時，通常都是階段高點。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXcS-6exHBSwlAA1QW7h4zGUSmZbWFgC47FLiSHztRKRwP9_vucCYblpY2XPEMotJzzkVmOfJYo5ts1hs5uGYAcbd9w_5VkgeZa6RYN9VzZmwZb_-VzPJwobbZJih9VnAfnzwZXF%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4dd08398&sv=2)

2024 / 10 CME smart money 由1,800張加倉至12,000張，這是有數據以來最大的持倉及加倉幅度，隨後BTC迎來單邊行情突破100K大關。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXf8nC-K0Fyg60DizkPxYnmFuOebnKbJvNvUDV_CnA9PKbXEXubjF-N0oEkA3sBJTzx8MY6IMLCMUtk00_xEP532s6evU_ao2JRCbiIGk1QPMW7em4emQKGEGf-hUXV1LtcgzVOV4A%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8af5b9d3&sv=2)

**使用須知**

感謝您使用 CoinKarma，本平台提供的數據指標主要基於過去的歷史表現，無法完全預測未來的市場走勢。加密貨幣市場具有高度的波動性，使用者應謹慎評估風險，並為自己的決策負責。

[PreviousCVD(Cumulative Volume Delta)](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/cvd-cumulative-volume-delta)
[NextBTC ETF Net Flow](https://docs.coinkarma.co/indicators-guide/btc-etf-net-flow)

# Custom Alerts | CoinKarma

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/features-guide/custom-alerts#shen-mo-shi-custom-alerts)

什麼是 Custom Alerts


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Custom Alerts 可以設置快訊通知，當指標達到自定義的閥值，系統會觸發快訊到 Telegram Bot，方便用戶偵測指標動態。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXc1CCiPocL7yxPK2oFPRFLwMoVz2sLjmt7p-XxmaAOR0T12pFK0t_AShNNe5jz-o5jMhKFKJybtYaWjSxJLzi2AYHLVAaREmFb7TnlXX3gXI7lX5i362BZrnIrJH7YeQvh5Cu64wA%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=930ecea6&sv=2)

[](https://docs.coinkarma.co/features-guide/custom-alerts#ru-he-she-ding-custom-alerts)

如何設定 Custom Alerts


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. 首先，完成 Telegram 帳戶的連結

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXctkvbvW1vLqzOgm7TlObIBJwvwTFKFldtB9TIOAR01MvKRTbxwsjyNTGexX7qHP9RcF6uIv_15lpgizNSYh64QWo70RGAYNv_erfZzDBcMpzWitosBEQY1jTf1UvN57HoOVNKG%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d8b459f&sv=2)

2\. 連結 Telegram 帳戶後，即可至設定中添加自定義出現快訊的條件。

![](https://docs.coinkarma.co/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Flh7-rt.googleusercontent.com%2Fdocsz%2FAD_4nXfjD_aAiwcILcmtfgzruddRO0zlAHvrXS_BsK-ooB9MttubKQOarwPwUfgQ7taAYO_PyWUqDV9e8cGrBm9JTZDBcn2nEw1RXZL_qnMY6kIETfZP1ByVDJM0TaG5AwyZZDKMYwsI%3Fkey%3DluLiz2GY4XjFT_nYY-mTIQJp&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c96a1729&sv=2)
